電影專刊好萊塢的姊妹花  華明　　在好萊塢有名的姊妹花狠多，像曼麗畢克馥之與洛黛畢克馥勞萊泰場之與波麗楊，諾瑪泰美琪之與康絲登泰美琪曼琳瑪許之與珍妮瑪許等等。但是能姊妹二人同在影壇上居重要地位的祇有康絲登裴納脫與瓊裴納脫姊妹二人了。現在所講的就是裴納脫一對姊妹花。在好萊塢圔家在銀幕上度藝術生活的除了巴里摩亞家族之外祇有裴納脫家族了。康絲登的父親名字呌李却裴納脫，李却早年時曾在銀壇上和舞臺上同時享過盛名的，祇因爲家產富有，中年時即抛棄藝術生涯。康絲登還有個姊姊名字呌做白蓓蘭裴納德，當初在英國度銀幕生活時曾馳名全歐州。後來到好萊塢也曾一度現身銀幕，到出嫁之後就和銀幕生活永别了。白蓓得意的時候康絲登祇十幾，歲而瓊還没滿十歲。康絲登父女姊妹四人各人享過盛名，但同時在一起享盛名的祇有康絲登和瓊二人在現在時候康絲登得名之後，瓊即由她姊姊領導之下得了名。有許多人說瓊完全是自已向前爬而没有經過康絲登的帮助，但是，康絲登當初未得名時受過多少頓挫失敗，而瓊竟能一帆風順，並没經過多大的頓挫失敗，可見瓊有康絲登做她的前車之鑒，不致再蹈同樣的覆轍，不能說不得益於康絲登。但是說這句話的也有他的理由。因爲康絲登和瓊二人的作風是完全不同的康絲登完全是個趨向奢華的女子的雛型，她的作風善於摹倣大家閨秀的劇烈之虚榮與難於馴從的有錢人的性格。而瓊裴納脫的作風完全是個柔弱女子的個性，熱烈和謙和的寫照，在她的近作（我倆婚史）一片中可以完全找出來。但是這種種祇可以說瓊裴納脫没有受她姊姊的影響，而不能說没有經過她姊姊的領導帮助。康絲登和瓊二人的感情極好，堪稱一對好姊妹，所以在二的感表上說，瓊不見得不受着康絲登的帮助吧。觀衆意見對（琵琶春怨）的貢獻  椀　　　　　　　（琵琶春怨）的中心思想，是描寫新舊兩方的矛盾，要算是寫實派的白描劇。但是牠的題名丨琵琶春怨丨有點牽强，似乎不足以代表全劇的精神，編劇者要把牠題名呌（琵琶春怨）就硬生生把墻上掛著一張琵琶，臨了呌不會彈琵琶的李令嫻，硬去彈一回，來凑合他的題目的暗射（琵琶别抱）的意思，這是多末勉强啊！說到導演方面，也有狠大的缺陷：就是盲母聽著她的兒子文小卿死去的消息之後，没有表現着十分悲痛的樣子。而且登時會放開笑臉來，聽令嫻彈琵琶！這一段情節，眞是荒乎其唐了。還有接吻一層，在本片中，固然是需要的；但是鄭小秋那一陣狂吻，似乎是太過火了吧？另外慕華在和李令嫻同居工作的時候，他的上衣，爲什麽始終不肯脫一下呢？本片的外景固然非常之好就是一切的裝飾陳設都狠合乎劇情不能不歸功於劉晉三君祇可惜用許多紙屑來做雪飛到人身上顯然一片一片的碎紙把眞實的雪景都弄假了未免畫蛇添足啊我對（花蝴蝶）的意見  李瓊　　本片的故事很簡單，在意識方面，談不上什麽，簡單的說，只是規勸青年努力事業，不要沉醉於酒色和不忠實於自已的愛情。男女主角表演都很不錯，如像喬治歌唱的時候，瑪麗對他的愛慕而感覺内心的愉快，同時喬治與却利刻苦練習武衛終於打倒了許多名手而得着了法國角力錦標的時候。瑪麗和喬治熱烈的狂吻之後，接着瑪麗便意識到將來的可怕而感受憂悒，因爲這時的喬治已爲巴黎的婦女們所注意，誰都想奪爲已有。這些地方都是表演得很動人的不過，不需要的穿插太多，使觀衆覺得有些厭煩。然而故事的結稱是說不大通的，瑪麗因喬治久不回家，竟决心與其離異，這一點未免將瑪利寫得太（超人）了。及喬治因困於洒色，自戕過甚，終於賽拳失敗，瑪麗乃復歸於喬治，而表示其愛之忠誠，固然，這些都是津津有味的但是將戀愛脫離經濟關係，而架空起來了。其他各方面，在技術上總算不壞，但也没有特别可取之處。（白金龍）前奏曲  培　　薛覺先的（白金龍）雖是從舞台上搬上銀幕，不個並非是整個的搬上銀幕，而是採取其中的精采部份和一些動人的有名影曲。現在：特將它的劇情簡述介紹如後：海上白家飯店小主人白金龍，因見有旅客白玉娘者，美艶多姿，不覺傾心。某日，白家飯店舉行化裝跳無會，玉娘亦參加，白欲與之舞，玉娘拒之，離坐至花園，白追至，責玉娘失禮，玉娘即反唇相譏，白雖遭玉娘奚落，然愛慕之心，曾不消减，後思得一計，乃於夜深人寂之時，白着全身黑服，帶面罩，立於玉娘室外，玉娘見窗幃上時現黑影，驚駭不能入睡，乃招茶役睡室外以伴，而茶役即白所喬裝者習日，而自訴衷曲，向玉娘求婚，玉娘責以青年應立志上進，不應持富妄爲，白受此敎訓後慚愧萬狀，乃立志赴南洋，作振興海外實業，後在星嘉坡與張晋華合辦大規模之橡皮廠，已任經理職，而張晋華即玉娘之父，故白金龍終得與玉娘成爲眷屬也。她們爲什麽不結婚  無懷　　（人猿泰山）的女主角摩蓮奥沙利文說：我對於愛這件事，覺得非常可怕，對於結婚呢，那更不必說了，我雖希望將來能結婚，不過至早要在我澈底大悟結婚的價值如何，意義如何，並對於人生有何等的需要之後。　　（蝴蝶夫人）的女主角薛爾維雪耐說：我喜歡結婚的！如其能依照我的方法丨我們已覺悟從前的女子爲靠丈夫而出嫁是不對的，倘我們結婚而不能達到我們所希望的，那末何必要使事情弄得更糟，而受人支配呢！我厭惡爲結婚而失去自由正像怕失掉我的財產一樣，我的不結婚，也許爲着這個原因吧，羅潑范來氏說：結婚簡直是沉淪女子的人格，我决不這樣做，他們的愛是在追求的時候，成功了就要想法來管朿你，我是不服他們管朿的。康斯登克明說：我對於結婚有些怕，因夫婦間往往爲着自利的緣故，閙出煩悶，若夫妻同是電影界的人更易因各地位的高低而生意見。看了（琵琶春怨）以後  松夫　　我們觀了明星改變作風的第一次出品（狂流），總算還能使我們觀衆說得一聲滿意，可是這第二次的出品（琵琶春怨），實在使我太失望了。（琵琶春怨）的故事，差不多完全是封建時代的思想，這影片的主旨，不外乎提倡女性的貞節，在新時代的流潮中，還有這種没落的影片出世，我眞要爲國片前途悲觀。講到導演方面，已並没有見到什麽進步，老實說（琵琶春怨）的導演，還不及李萍情先生第一次的作品（舊恨新慾）呢。演員的表情，鄭小秋的小鬍子最使我難堪，化裝很是惡劣，高倩蘋的表演，很是平平，張敏玉是有表現天才的小明星，前途是很有希望的。總之，使我滿意的只有剪接，佈景，攝影，三者而已。我希望明星今後在出品上，再不要像這類没落的封建思想底影片，還是向（狂流）那作風般的影片努力吧。天一影訊  菁主　　（女工程師）改做（生機）　　天一一九三三年巨片（女工程師），在邵醉翁導演底下，由陳玉梅，胡珊袁美雲主演，現在趕緊工作，業已拍去了幾個塲面了。但是，連日來導演邵醉翁氏一方面固然忙該片的佈景，是印咸和新近進入公司的許幸之担任。於把（女工程師）開拍，另一方面則在忙於把劇本修改，并且决定把（女工程師）改做生機；劇本中的一幕偉構無線電工廠也决意改爲女縫衣工塲了，其他的劇情，也有許多修改的地方。趙靜霞重上銀幕　  墨客　　趙靜霞自脫離明星公司後，息影多時，雖受大華之聘，但大華始終未拍一戲，去夏趙曾在新新公司後面創設安樂冷飲部，因開支浩大，致未可赢餘，近悉顧無爲之大華公司攝影塲，俟强華公司范雪明之戲攝完，卽進行一無聲片，而與觀衆闊别多日之趙靜霞，也於此時重上銀幕和觀衆相見矣。電影小說紅塵（ＲｅｄＤｕｓｔ（二）  桀克暴風過去已是向晚，但尼斯和麥克騎着滿身灰汗的髒馬，跟着裝滿橡皮和苦力的牛車，沿着河旁一條高低不平的泥土路，行向宅塲而去。他們來到宅塲的時候已是滿地月色，牛車和苦力回他們的老家，但尼斯和麥克一直到了宅塲廊前下馬，但尼斯喊（居同！）没有一點動靜。他們就在廊下靜靜地洗了手面，但尼斯走進臥室，麥克跟着。居同在桌旁一張靠背椅上懶洋洋躺着，顯已失了知覺。但尼斯揪住他的地髮，打他兩下耳光，居同微微的一聲，但是仍舊不張開眼睛。但尼斯就同麥克把這失了知感的人抬到他的房間！沿着陽臺一排房間中的一個，也没有停下來點燈，他們就重重的把他丢在床上。（噲！什麽意思？黑暗中來了一個聲音！一個驚悖的聲音！一個急促的聲音！一個女人的聲音！但尼斯把電筒一照，注視着這婦人在床上掙扎坐起。麥克見她很年輕，就趕快去把燈點着，以便細看，她兩眼雖充滿着一種恨毒的珨俐，她飽滿的嘴唇雖則帶着輕輕的曲綫，她是年輕呀！年輕！可愛！美麗的鬆髮！但尼斯不動情的對她看着，（您在這衷做什？）他問。（猜猜看　　）這婦人給他慢慢的有意思的一瞥。（我知道），但尼斯厲聲的說，（您是從西貢乘船來的！同着他，是不是？）（請你把他抬出去，好不好？）這婦人說着，對那懶臥在床沿上的人，恨恨的一看，脚一伸，她把居同推到地板上去了，他咕嚕一聲，又像一團爛泥了。（您對他覺得那　樣子，那您又何必離開西貢呢？）但尼斯淡淡的問。（他答允我五百個法郎，）這婦人說，（現在我要這筆錢，急急平要，我至今没有看見這錢，）她又說，同時對着二人一看。你不會看見這筆錢的，）但尼斯直捷了當的告訴她，（他能不能有五十個法郎，我還不相信，）（怎麽！撤謊！好，任憑什樣，我現在要洗心革面！）她向下看看這泥醉的管事，（他要呌隨便什麽女子幹那事的，我要去！）（那條船四星期裏是不再來的，）麥克揷嘴說，看就情形很有意味。（不要挖苦！）這女子覺得不自在，然她聳一聳肩，（好的，這好像我葉丹在鄕憇忽！我常常喜歡旅行！旅行遇着些新人！看那一半的人生是怎樣的！）說完了的時候她受了震動的一雙緣眼向着但尼斯一閃。他轉了身說，一麥克，走罷）。（噲！）　丹向着他們喊，（你們是不是要把他丢在這裏？）（那是他的房間，爲什麽呢？）但尼斯答覆她。（請！帶他出去！）這女子向他們堅請着說，（我要睡覺！這地方盡是斷蜴蟑螂！）（未完）

1933.03.20

Xifengkou 1

Liu's Troops Launch a Two-Pronged Attack 2

The Center of Battle Shifts to the Left Flank 3

After Li's Brigade Conducted a Night Raid on the Enemy's Rear Positions, Killing Five to Six Hundred and Capturing Many Machine Guns, Our Side Suffered Heavy Casualties; a Battalion Commander Died Heroically. No Enemy Traces Were Found Ten Miles Outside of Luowenyu.

Beiping - Our troops at Luowenyu, supervised by Liu Ruming last night, launched a two-pronged attack and engaged the enemy fiercely in the vicinity of a crossroads. The battle continued until 2:00 AM this morning. Over a hundred enemies were killed and more than twenty were captured. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - The 29th Army's Beiping Office received a phone call from the front this afternoon stating that there were no clashes on the main front at Xifengkou, and the center of the battle had shifted to the Luowenyu area on the left flank. On the evening of the 18th, Liu sent Li Jintian's brigade to bypass seven mountain peaks to the enemy's rear, advancing to the enemy's machine gun positions. A simultaneous frontal attack resulted in a bloody battle, killing five to six hundred enemy soldiers and capturing more than ten heavy machine guns, bringing back six and destroying five. Currently, there are no enemy traces ten miles outside Luowenyu. In this battle, Wang, the battalion commander of our 38th Division, bravely led the charge, sustaining severe injuries but continuing to shout slogans to kill the enemy. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - The Staff Office of Liu Ruming's Division received a phone call this morning stating that over three thousand enemies, a mixed force of infantry, cavalry, and artillery from Shanzhagang and Shabogang, with more than thirty field guns and thirty machine guns, were met head-on by the division commander himself leading the 1st Regiment's pistol squad in three teams, engaging in a bloody battle for a whole day and night starting at 1:00 AM on the 18th. At 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 18th, the 1st Brigade Commander, Li Jintian, was ordered to lead the entire 2nd Regiment and pistol squad to reinforce, launching three assaults and killing hundreds of enemies. By 2:00 AM on the morning of the 19th, the enemy's artillery fire was sparse. In addition to killing over a thousand officers and soldiers, the remaining enemies have been completely surrounded between the two hills. If there are no major reinforcements coming, it will not be difficult to annihilate them soon. Our Regiment Commander Li once bravely sustained injuries, and two company commanders of the 1st Battalion were killed in action. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - A phone call from Santunying states that the enemies at Luowenyu and Shanzhayu, after being fiercely attacked by our army for two days and nights, with a force of eight to nine thousand, have all been defeated and are retreating towards Banbishan this morning. The fiercest fighting occurred on the night of the 18th, with heavy artillery densely shelling our positions. Our army was temporarily caught in a difficult situation due to the intense enemy artillery fire. Division Commander Liu Ruming sent Wang, the battalion commander of the 38th Division's Special Service Battalion, leading the entire battalion of soldiers to charge and kill behind the enemy lines. The enemy, fearing an attack on their rear, had arranged machine gun teams in formation. Our troops mistakenly entered the enemy's machine gun positions. Gunfire suddenly erupted in the front, and our troops rolled into the enemy's machine gun positions, eventually killing five to six hundred enemies, breaking through the positions, and causing the enemy's front to waver and collapse. In this battle, our casualties were about two companies, and eleven enemy machine guns were captured. Battalion Commander Wang also died heroically. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - Zhang Jifan telegraphed from the 17th, stating that the Japanese 31st Regiment, which had been attacking us for days, camped in the vicinity of Kuaipailin last night. This morning at 8:00 AM, the enemy launched a major assault on our Luowenyu and Shanzhayukou. Our Division Commander Liu Ruming supervised his troops in resistance. The enemy gathered at Dapo and attacked our Dongjiakou this morning but were repelled by our defending soldiers. Small numbers of enemies also attacked our positions at Tiemenguan and Panjiakou and were all repelled. There were no changes on the main front at Xifengkou. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - Song Zheyuan skillfully telegraphed to Beiping, stating that after the enemy who attacked our Luowenyu and Shanzhayu area was fiercely attacked by us last night, they increased their forces this morning and launched a vigorous counterattack under concentrated artillery fire. Our defending soldiers occupied various key passes of the Great Wall, calmly fighting back with machine guns and grenades. The enemy ultimately failed to succeed. According to reliable reports, the enemy's newly arrived mixed brigades and the 33rd Regiment are advancing towards us along the Shahe River this morning, and their vanguard has reached the vicinity of Banbishan. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - Zhang Weifan telegraphed to Beiping, stating that after the remnants of the enemy Hattori Brigade on the main front at Xifengkou were defeated by us, the enemy retreated to mountain peaks further away from the pass. There have been no major clashes on the main front in recent days, and the focus of the battle has shifted to the Luowenyu area. On the evening of the 18th, Division Commander Liu Ruming ordered Li Jintian's brigade to conduct a night raid on the front line, advancing in two wings. One part bypassed through Shaziyu to the enemy's rear, crossing seven mountain peaks to reach the enemy's machine gun positions. The enemy was killed and wounded by broadswords, five to six hundred in total, and the entire line collapsed. There are no enemy traces ten miles outside of Luowenyu. Our 29th Army has suffered five to six thousand casualties, most of whom are being cared for by the local residents of Zunhua and Tongxian counties. Farmers from various villages have come to offer condolences. Some of the wounded soldiers have been sent to Beiping for treatment and are being accommodated by the Support Association and various organizations. The fresh troops of a certain division of our army arrived at Malanguan at noon on the 19th, deploying along the Great Wall, solidifying defenses and greatly boosting military morale. Song Zheyuan appointed Qi Guangyuan as the Commander of Zunhua City Defense, responsible for the defense of Zunhua. (19th Dispatch)

Tianjin - A telegram from the front states that after the enemy advancing on Luowenyu and Shanzhayu was fiercely attacked by us on the night of the 17th, they increased their forces on the morning of the 18th, concentrating artillery fire to cover their counterattack. Our defending soldiers occupied various key passes of the Great Wall, fighting back with machine guns and grenades. As of the evening of the 18th, fierce fighting was still ongoing. According to reports, the enemy's newly arrived mixed brigades and the 32nd Regiment were advancing towards us along the Chehe River on the afternoon of the 18th and have reached the vicinity of Bandishan. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - A certain unit of our fresh troops arrived at a certain key pass of the Great Wall fifty miles north of Zunhua this morning, greatly boosting military morale. Small enemy units were discovered at small passes such as Tiemenying and Panjiakou yesterday and were defeated by our defending soldiers. Yesterday, a large part of the enemy attacked our Dongjiakou but were repelled by our Regiment Commander Liu, and the enemy retreated to Dapo. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - Liu Ruming telegraphed to Beiping on the 18th, stating that mixed enemy forces of infantry, cavalry, and artillery, numbering about three to four thousand, carrying twenty machine guns and field guns each, launched attacks on Luowenyu, Shanzhakou, and Shaboyu early yesterday morning. He led the Li Zengzhi Regiment and two Special Service Battalions to engage the enemy, fighting fiercely for a day and night, killing hundreds of enemies and capturing ten. Regiment Commander Li bravely sustained injuries but did not retreat. The fighting was fiercest at Shanzhakou, and our Liu Fuxiang Battalion suffered heavier casualties. The enemy is already struggling to hold on. (19th Dispatch)

Beiping - Wang Shuqing and Cui Shulin, the company commanders of Song's troops who captured sixteen cannons at Laoposhan outside Xifengkou, arrived in Beiping injured this morning. Company Commander Wang has only twenty-four men remaining, and Company Commander Cui has eighteen, with the rest having died heroically. Cui, being a fellow villager, saw a streetcar in the city and actually said, "Why is the train entering the city?" Song's troops recently captured many spies, all remnants of Tang's forces, identified by wearing woolen underwear. It is claimed that the Japanese are buying them off, paying two hundred yuan per month, with an extra two yuan per day when they set out, disguised as woodcutters, to plot disturbances in various places. (19th Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan's Army Suffers Several Thousand Casualties 4

Beiping - Our 29th Army has been fighting fiercely for ten days, and total casualties have reached five to six thousand. Most of the wounded soldiers are being accommodated and treated in Zunhua North Tongzhou, and some have been sent to Beiping. (19th Dispatch)

Enemies at Malanyu are Repelled 5

Tianjin - The enemies discovered at Malanyu have been repelled by our army. (19th Dispatch)

Enemy General Will Use 50,000 Troops to Avenge the Defeats 6

Tianjin - Song's army has been fighting bloody battles against the Japanese outside Xifengkou for ten days. Although morale is high, the troops are exhausted. They are urgently awaiting the arrival of reinforcements so that they can rest. An enemy general plans to use 50,000 troops to attack Xifengkou in order to avenge their repeated defeats. (19th Dispatch)

Duan Sends Personnel to the Front to Offer Condolences 7

Tianjin - Duan Qirui in Shanghai, upon hearing that Song Zheyuan's army had repeatedly defeated the stubborn enemy, was extremely gratified. On the 18th, he telegraphed Tianjin, asking Wang Yitang and others to purchase goods and send personnel to the front to offer condolences. (19th Dispatch)

Enemy's Main Force Attacks Shanzhayukou 8

Beiping - Zhang Weifan telegraphed from the 17th, stating that today the enemy launched an attack on our Luowenyu with a part of their forces, and were met head-on by Qi Guangyuan's regiment, resulting in many enemy casualties. At the same time, the enemy launched a major assault on our Shanzhayukou positions with their main force, engaging in close combat with Liu Ruming's Division's Li Zengzhi Regiment in a bloody battle all day long. Our Regiment Commander Li was injured while supervising the battle, and other officers and soldiers also suffered many casualties. According to prisoners of war, the enemy is composed of the 31st Regiment and a part of the 8th Regiment, along with Mongolian and Korean puppet troops, totaling eight to nine thousand men, accompanied by fifty trucks, three armored vehicles, and five aircraft, and is a newly arrived fresh force rerouted from Chaoyang and Pingquan. (19th Dispatch)

Japanese Aircraft Bomb Our Rear Positions 9

Beiping - A phone call from Shixiazhen states that the Japanese military's defensive works at Gubeikou seem to have been constructed. Most of the Japanese troops are moving towards Xifengkou. Enemy aircraft have been conducting reconnaissance and bombing in the rear positions for days. (19th Dispatch)

Various Parties Send Telegrams to Comfort Song and Sun 10

Beiping - Bai Chongxi, Dai Ji, Kong Xiangxi, and others have sent telegrams to comfort Song and Sun. (19th Dispatch)

Song Zheyuan's Troops Endure Hardships Alone 11

Beiping - Qin Dechun wrote a letter to his friends in Beiping on the 17th, stating that fierce fighting has been ongoing here for ten days, and we endure hardships alone, causing great anxiety. The enemy attacking our Xifengkou has been quieter in the past two days after being fiercely attacked by our army. However, starting from the 16th, new enemy reinforcements of about a mixed brigade, consisting of the Japanese 31st Fleet and the 8th Regiment, were transferred from Chengde to Luowenyukou and Shanzhayukou, twenty miles north of Zunhua. The fighting with Liu Ruming's Division has been extremely fierce for two days. The enemy is attempting to cut off our army's lines of communication with Beiping. In the fight for the mountain peaks on the left flank of Luowenyu, our soldiers are charging forward and being cut down from behind, with corpses lying everywhere, but their spirit has not diminished slightly. The enemy has suffered even greater losses. Three of the enemy's companies have been completely annihilated by our army. Our Regiment Commander Zengzhi Li was wounded in the thigh at 5:00 PM this afternoon but continued to supervise the battle despite his injuries. Division Commander Ruming Liu personally braved bullets and artillery fire, bravely killing the enemy. Lord Song is determined to resist to the end, personally going to the front lines every day to supervise and inspect. Your brother also accompanies him. According to reports, the enemy has mobilized more than two thousand additional troops from Chengde, consisting of mixed Japanese, Mongolian, and Korean forces. It is expected that they will arrive at our positions tomorrow morning, and there will be a bloody battle. (19th Dispatch)

Messenger Bravely Kills Enemies 12

Beiping - Cui Lianyou's messenger, a young boy, was surrounded and searched by Japanese soldiers while delivering orders at Laoposhan. The young boy said, "Don't search me, I'll take off my clothes myself." After speaking, he drew a pistol and fired wildly, taking the enemy soldiers by surprise, killing seven. The remaining one chased and shot the young boy, wounding him. He was rescued by Song's troops and sent to Tongzhou Hospital for treatment. He Yingqin, recognizing his loyalty and bravery, ordered him to be transported to Beiping for treatment on the 19th. (19th Dispatch)

Current Commentary 13

The Impending Storm in the European Political Situation 14

Since the unprecedented panic in international capitalism in 1929, four years have passed with the situation deteriorating daily. Complaints resonate throughout the universe, and a sense of depression covers the world. In this cloudy and rainless period, people of the world are eager for catharsis, and the clear and bright days will eventually be seen again after a baptism of fierce winds and storms. This is inevitable due to the inherent nature of things.

Since the sudden outbreak of the September 18th Incident, the situation in the Far East has become increasingly urgent. The economic panic and social unrest have prompted Japanese imperialism to launch an intensified invasion of China, and this invasion has spurred the Chinese national anti-imperialist struggle. Although this struggle has been obstructed by domestic reactionary forces from time to time, the broad anti-imperialist revolution in Asia will eventually erupt from the Sino-Japanese conflict. This has been determined by historical trends and economic conditions and cannot be reversed by any human power. Recently, the rise of the reactionary regime in Germany has suddenly made the European atmosphere tense, and a second world war is imminent.

The second world war will be a conflict between imperialist powers, not a unified struggle against the Soviet Union. The start of the conflict between imperialist powers, with Europe, known for its developed nationalism, as its fuse, has long been foreseen by insightful individuals. The development of the situation in continental Europe in recent months has fully proven the correctness of this judgment. The anti-Soviet front in Europe was originally centered on France, with the Little Entente as its claws and teeth. Although conflicts between Britain and the Soviet Union occurred repeatedly, the frequent changes of government in Britain and the relationship between Britain and France, where two powers could not stand together, meant that the British policy towards Soviet Russia was always in a state of seeming closeness and detachment, sometimes separating and sometimes uniting. Germany and Italy, on the other hand, often maintained friendly relations with the Soviet Union due to their hostility towards France. The recent shift in the situation began during Papen's tenure in Germany. At that time, although the National Socialist Party had not yet seized power, it already had an irresistible force. In order to gain national sympathy and show goodwill to the National Socialist Party, Papen publicly proposed the demand for equality in armaments. As the German nationalistic movement intensified and Italy's momentum became increasingly aggressive, France, feeling threatened from within, had to shift its focus to dealing with Italy and Germany. France and the Little Entente then jointly signed non-aggression treaties with the Soviet Union, and the so-called anti-Soviet front disappeared.

In recent days, the power of the German National Socialist Party has been temporarily stabilized, and the anti-French united front of Italy, Germany, and Austria has become increasingly clear. The Italian arms shipment to Austria has aroused the joint protest of Britain and France, and border disputes between Germany and Poland, and Germany and France have also reappeared. The European war clouds are spreading, and a single spark could ignite a major conflict. At this time, British Prime Minister MacDonald suddenly went to Geneva and proposed his so-called five-year disarmament plan. Before Hitler went to Italy, he personally visited Rome to meet with Mussolini, using high-sounding arguments to win the sympathy of those who are living in fantasy. This has always been a common technique of individualistic gentlemen in Europe and America. To use the opportunity to obtain European hegemony through diplomatic strategies is also a long-held ambition of the British Empire. MacDonald's efforts can only be explained in this way. However, the so-called five-year disarmament plan is empty and meaningless. To try to save the dying disarmament conference with it is just a dream. The plan has already aroused criticism from both France and Germany. To try to reconcile the two parties and instead be opposed by both is almost inevitable. In the future, will Britain try to unite with Italy to control France and Germany? Then the question of who will hold European hegemony will become the focus of the struggle between Britain and Italy. We only feel that it will increase the conflict and not help the reality.

In addition to the tense international situation in Europe, the internal crises of various countries are also intensifying. Within a month, newspapers have reported events such as the resignation of officials in Spain, Poland, and Romania, a naval mutiny in the Netherlands, and demonstrations by hundreds of thousands of unemployed people in Britain. All of these indicate that the continuous line of social revolution has accelerated its density. All changes in history begin with tentative efforts that appear to be interrupted, leading to an all-out struggle. Therefore, from a social historical perspective, the occurrence of social revolution has already been in motion long before today. However, its intensification must be given time. The dictatorship of the German National Socialist Party will cause the domestic Communist Party to shift from open and peaceful political participation to secret and violent uprisings, and the compromising centrists will shift from illusory wandering to extremist fronts. This is also a desperate move forced by circumstances. From this, the division of the struggle will become more obvious, and the actions of the struggle will become more intense. To think that German society will enter a smooth path from here is truly blind and superficial.

Enemy Plans to Invade Eastern Hebei and Tianjin 15

Beiping - After the Hattori and Suzuki brigades of the enemy forces suffered setbacks in attacking Xifengkou, they began to shift their main force to attack Luowenyu on the 15th, attempting to attack Zunhua in order to flank the main front at Xifengkou. Division Commander Liu Ruming led his troops to engage the enemy, and after three days and nights of fighting, annihilated many enemy soldiers and almost completely resolved the enemy at Luowenyu, causing the enemy's second plan to fail. The enemy, having suffered repeated setbacks, plans to concentrate their main force within days and launch a simultaneous attack from the main front at Xifengkou and various passes west of Tongxian, attempting a large-scale attack. It is expected that there will be a major battle within a day or two. It is said that if the enemy attacks again and fails to capture Xifengkou, they plan to invade eastern Hebei on one hand and disrupt Tianjin and Beiping on the other, in order to achieve their goals. However, our side is fully prepared, and if the enemy attacks, we will resolutely deal them a head-on blow. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Comments from a certain military expert

First Grand Gathering Since the European War 51

British and Italian Prime Ministers in Heart-to-Heart Talks

Solving Political Problems That Endanger the International Situation　　Depends on Close Cooperation Between the World's Major Powers

Reuters, Rome, 18th. British Prime Minister MacDonald and others arrived in Italy from Geneva by train, got off at Genoa, and changed to a plane to Rome, arriving six hours earlier than scheduled. Traveling day and night without rest shows that the British Prime Minister is eager to solve the major problems Europe has recently encountered. As soon as the British Prime Minister arrived here, he had a preliminary discussion with Mussolini at the Italian Prime Minister's official residence regarding the current situation. The first meeting between the two Prime Ministers lasted a long time and was unexpected. It started at 6 p.m. and ended after 8 p.m. The content of the conversation was not announced.

British and Italian Positions Are Generally Consistent 52

However, it is expected that the British Prime Minister will explain in detail his disarmament plan presented in Geneva on Thursday, because the British Prime Minister's proposal published in Italian newspapers is quite brief. After arriving in Rome, the British Prime Minister told people that although he only attended the Geneva Disarmament Conference for a few days this week, he realized that political and other difficult problems endangering the international situation do need to be resolved quickly. To get rid of the difficulties, we can only rely on close cooperation between the world's major powers. All Italian newspapers tonight also stated that there should be close cooperation between the major powers, and hope that after the meeting between the British and Italian Prime Ministers, the authorities of the major powers will immediately gather for discussions one after another.

Comprehensive Discussion of European Issues 53

Tonight, the Italian Prime Minister held a grand banquet at his official residence to entertain the British Prime Minister. This is the first grand gathering since the European War. It is heard that in addition to the disarmament issue, the British Prime Minister will inquire about Italy's attitude towards German Fascism after Hitler's assumption of the prime ministership, and the Balkan issue, including the dangerous situation in Yugoslavia, may also be discussed. There is no doubt that the World Economic Conference will also be discussed. Tomorrow, Sunday, a meeting will be held at the British Embassy to continue the discussion of everything. The Italian Prime Minister will have lunch at the American Embassy and meet with British Foreign Minister Simon.

British Prime Minister Granted Audience with the Pope and the Italian King 54

Reuters, Rome, 18th. British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon are very busy here. This morning, Mr. MacDonald was granted an audience with the Italian King, and then the Italian King gave a banquet. Mr. MacDonald's daughter was also present. In the afternoon, Mr. MacDonald and Mr. Simon continued to talk with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini until 6:30 in the evening when the time for an audience with the Pope arrived before they dispersed. The two British politicians claimed today that yesterday's talks with the Italian Prime Minister were very satisfactory. It is heard that the main issue currently being discussed is the possibility of reaching an understanding on the four-power consultation. This understanding is mainly based on Britain and Italy, and France and Germany are expected to participate. The revision of the treaty is also a major event for discussion, because the Italian Prime Minister believes that unless this move is successful, and the current mutual suspicion between France and Germany is eliminated, and the inferior position of the former enemy countries today is improved, there will be no progress in Europe. However, the Italian Prime Minister has solemnly stated that this kind of revision must be based on mutual agreement and must not be carried out by force. Mr. MacDonald was relieved to hear this.

Italian Chamber of Deputies Filled with Cheers 55

Havas, Rome, 18th. When Prime Minister Mussolini entered the Chamber of Deputies, the entire venue was filled with cheers. This expression seems to be related to the arrival of the British authorities in Rome.

Good Impression of German Public Opinion 56

National, Berlin, 18th. German public opinion has a very good impression of British Prime Minister MacDonald's visit to Italian Prime Minister Mussolini this time. The Deutsche Allgemeine Zeitung stated that these two are both heads of state of a country, and both have made achievements in unifying the country. From a political point of view, the positions of the two are also equal, because they do not represent socialism, nor are they capitalists, but are representatives of the new era. Therefore, the meeting between the two can guarantee that they will be harmonious and unhindered, and the revival of Europe depends on the cooperation of these two.

French Newspapers Viciously Defame MacDonald 57

National, Paris, 18th. Today, the Paris Daily News, in discussing the return of French Prime Minister Daladier and Foreign Minister Pengu from Geneva, viciously scolded the British Prime Minister and his new disarmament plan, considering it to be treacherous and hypocritical, willing to sacrifice all countries in the world, while Britain alone benefits. The newspaper's editorial also attacked MacDonald, claiming that MacDonald considers himself an arbitrator and orders France and other Allied countries in the European War to disarm together. It ended by saying that MacDonald's intention was nothing more than to promote the re-signing of the peace treaty.

Herriot Urges France to Be Cautious 58

Havas, Marseilles, France, 18th. Herriot, the party leader of the Radical Socialist Party (the current ruling party) and former Prime Minister, published an article in the Petit Provençal, discussing the draft disarmament convention proposed by British Prime Minister MacDonald, stating that France is under close surveillance at this time and must be extremely cautious. The main principle of the British plan is to engage in disarmament, and not to re-compete in armaments. Mr. Herriot believes that this principle is very good. As for how this plan will be implemented, Mr. Herriot will only express his opinion after he fully understands how the international supervision system will be organized. Regarding the military quotas of various countries, the British plan has set numbers for all of them, but it has never mentioned the military quota that Britain should have. Mr. Herriot finds this quite strange. As for the so-called consultation treaty, Mr. Herriot believes that it is still questionable whether the United States can agree to it. Mr. Herriot also said that the newspapers of the German nationalist faction oppose the British plan and are propagating quite vigorously.

Reuters, Geneva, 18th. The first official reaction to the disarmament agreement proposed by British Prime Minister MacDonald on Thursday has come from the Little Entente. It is expected that this aspect will have a great influence on the future success of the British proposal. The Time Is Ripe for the Resumption of Diplomatic Relations Between the United States and Russia 62

The Japanese Foreign Ministry Takes Preemptive Action

Engaging in Treaty Negotiations with Russia

Washington. Today, those close to the White House indicated that the day the United States recognizes Soviet Russia is very close. If there is no banking crisis, President Roosevelt may recommend this matter to the Senate this week. According to the Department of Commerce, the actual value of the US dollar has returned to the value before March 3. It is expected that the issue of recognizing Soviet Russia will be raised soon. It is heard that someone has suggested two strategies to the President: one is to first sign a commercial treaty, and the other is to immediately recognize the Russian government and then resolve commercial matters through formal diplomatic channels. The President's attitude is quite inclined towards the second strategy, but a firm decision has not yet been made. It is expected that there will be positive progress in the next few weeks. It is also heard that the recognition procedure will probably imitate the first agreement between Britain and Russia, stipulating that neither side shall engage in propaganda, and then exchange ambassadors, and then discuss commercial treaties, or even the debt issues of the Tsarist era. The main reason for this attitude of the US government is to promote the US goods market. The long-standing advocacy of resuming diplomatic relations with Russia by key members of the Democratic Party is secondary. However, no matter what procedure the US President adopts, it must first be approved by the Senate. Currently, the new senators in the Senate have not yet expressed their opinions. It is only heard that the recognition proposal can find the support of the majority. Among the 51 old senators, 22 firmly support recognition, 20 are still unwilling to express a clear attitude, and only 9 openly oppose it. Moreover, among them, only one, Copeland, held an opposing position before taking office in the new government, and now claims that he will vote in favor for the sake of commerce. The current Secretary of the Navy, Swanson, is also one of the supporters. When he was a senator, he pointed out that a new treaty should be signed everywhere before recognition, and the President can select an ambassador, who can go to the US after being approved by the Senate. As for the treaty, it may be negotiated later. (18th National Dispatch) Tokyo. According to a report from the Japanese Ambassador to the United States, the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs said that the new US government will adopt a new diplomatic policy towards Russia, and it is heard that it has decided to recognize Russia. In the eyes of the public, it can be said that the US recognition of Soviet Russia is a foregone conclusion, but it has been delayed for several weeks due to the domestic financial panic. There are two forms of recognition: one is to sign a commercial treaty with Russia and give it substantive recognition, and the other is to announce formal recognition and formally negotiate and sign all treaties required in diplomacy at the same time. According to speculation in the public, the United States will adopt the second form, which can be realized in these few weeks. The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs believes that the approach between the US and Russia is very inconvenient for Japan's policy of dominating Asia, and has decided to hinder it in various ways. It is rumored that the non-aggression treaty between Russia and Japan will enter a new stage. (19th China United News Agency Dispatch)

Tokyo. Sakou Hideichi, a councilor of the Japanese Embassy in Russia, went west this afternoon. Since the Soviet Russian side requested negotiations to promote Japanese-Russian economic relations after taking office, preparations must be made. Therefore, he took a counterproposal this time and will cooperate with Ambassador Ota. In the event of substantial negotiations, Sakou's activities in Soviet Russia are extremely noteworthy. Those arrested are all people who have legitimate occupations in commerce, are self-disciplined, and have no grievances with others. It is strange to say that such people would participate in any conspiracy that would destroy their own lives." What kind of motives are behind Soviet Russia's arbitrary arrest of British people? I have no way of knowing here, but I know that previous governments have deliberately created external difficulties in order to divert their people's attention from domestic events. If Russia's real purpose is here, then I dare say that the British people will never be deceived by it. Commercial relations must be based on mutual benefit. If we want to facilitate commercial relations, we must not allow this relationship to be subject to undue obstacles. Although we do not approve of Soviet Russia's political goals, we have always expressed our desire not to interfere in Soviet Russia's internal affairs. If Soviet Russia believes that the commercial and diplomatic relations that both sides need can continue when British people are being trampled on by them, then they are greatly mistaken." Hitler's Unification Succeeds 93

New German Parliament to Convene Tomorrow

The Opening Ceremony Will Be Solemn and Grand

Proclamation to the Nation to Hang New Flags

Berlin, 18th (National News Agency) – The new German Parliament is scheduled to convene at the Potsdam Garrison Church on Tuesday. Preparations are actively underway to celebrate the grand occasion, with the aim of awakening the German people's admiration for the glory of the past empire. The newly appointed Minister of Propaganda, Mr. Goering, also issued a (proclamation to the people of the nation) today, stating that the new members of Parliament will gather in the sacred place where the ancient kings of Prussia rest, to declare the German people's belief in unity and freedom. Since the founding of Germany, internal division has been the poison of the nation. Today, for the first time in history, the people of the nation can concentrate their strength, overcome internal disputes, and unite various ethnic groups, classes, and beliefs under a unified government. Germany has now awakened and calls upon the people to hang the glorious black, white, and red national emblem and the 卐 flag on the day of the Parliament's reconvening, to express the people's deep faith in the rebirth of the nation. In addition, the Ministry of the Interior has issued a notice ordering the entire nation to hang the new national flag and the 卐 flag on the day the new Parliament convenes. All civil servants will be given a day off, all schools will be closed for a day, and the Ministry of National Defense has scheduled a military parade at noon on that day. The national anthem will be played and a 21-gun salute will be fired throughout the country that morning. The Ministry of Aviation has also declared an air curfew on that day, prohibiting all aircraft from flying over Berlin and Potsdam. As for the opening of the Parliament, President Hindenburg will deliver an address, after which Hitler will announce his major policies. At this time, President Hindenburg will step down and go alone to the front of the tombs of former Prussian Kings Frederick William I and Frederick the Great to lay a wreath.

German President Grants Hitler 94

Special Powers for Financial Reform

Berlin, 18th (National News) – Today, the German President issued an order granting the Hitler Cabinet great powers to implement financial reforms and assist the poor and middle class, including significant powers over taxes, relief funds, and domestic debt. Even the power to increase or decrease the silver content in currency is granted. The government is also authorized to lend 30 million marks to the middle-class trade loan association. Monitoring the Colombia-Peru Dispute 95

League of Nations Forms Advisory Committee

US Government Approves Geneva Action

Believes It Does Not Conflict with the Monroe Doctrine

Geneva, 18th (Havas) – The Advisory Committee organized by the League of Nations Administrative Council to monitor the Peru-Colombia dispute is composed of representatives from the following countries: (1) Germany, (2) Great Britain, (3) China, (4) Spain, (5) France, (6) Guatemala, (7) Ireland, (8) Italy, (9) Mexico, (10) Norway, (11) Panama, (12) Romania, (13) Czechoslovakia. In addition, it is planned to invite the United States and Brazil to participate in the work of the committee.

Washington, 18th (National News) – Today, the US State Department issued a statement to the press stating that the US government has no objections to the League of Nations' actions in providing a basis for resolving the Leticia dispute between Peru and Colombia, and to the resolutions of the League of Nations Administrative Council. Yesterday, the League of Nations Administrative Council passed the report of the special committee on the Leticia case, recommending that maintaining the sanctity of existing treaties be the basis for resolution, and organized a 13-nation advisory committee to monitor its progress. At that time, many representatives believed that this move by the League of Nations could be regarded as the end of the Monroe Doctrine. Therefore, the US government issued a statement today to dispel this view, reiterating the US government's attitude towards the Monroe Doctrine, stating that the Monroe Doctrine is clearly a US policy to prevent Europeans from colonizing the Western Hemisphere. The US government has used this policy to prevent Europeans from interfering in the internal affairs of Western Hemisphere countries. Therefore, the Monroe Doctrine cannot be applied to the resolutions of international organizations such as the League of Nations regarding international issues related to member states. Since most Latin American republics are members of the League of Nations, the Monroe Doctrine naturally cannot be applied to the resolutions of the League of Nations. Observers of diplomacy also said that this explanation by the State Department has not changed the US's historical attitude towards the Monroe Doctrine, and is consistent with President Wilson's declaration. Wilson once said that this doctrine only requires European countries not to attempt to expand their political systems to the west of the Atlantic. Former Secretary of the Navy Swanson also stated during the Senate debate on joining the International Court of Justice that the Monroe Doctrine is a US policy, and in practice is a political policy, not international law. As of today, figures from both the Democratic and Republican parties in Congress acknowledge that the resolutions of the League of Nations Administrative Council are not an attempt to interfere in the internal affairs of Peru and Colombia, nor an attempt to impose European political concepts on these two countries.

US Treasury Drafts Regulations 96

Severe Punishment for Hoarding Gold

Large Sums of Cash Shipped to Italy

Washington, 10th (Reuters) – President Roosevelt has approved state authorities to send personnel to manage state banks that are members of the Federal Reserve System. These banks can only open after the Treasury Department grants licenses. The list of names of people who withdrew large sums of cash from banks before the bank holiday has been sent to the Federal Reserve, which will review them in detail and then transfer them to the Treasury Department. The Treasury Department is currently drafting regulations to punish hoarders. The proposed measures are said to be quite severe.

New York, 18th (Reuters) – According to information obtained by the financial reporters of the New York American, US cash worth 8.5 million yuan has obtained a special license from the Treasury Department to be shipped to Italy. This cash was withdrawn from reserves long ago and listed in the accounts of Italian banks. This is the first batch of cash shipped out since President Roosevelt's gold ban. Once this precedent is set, foreign gold worth 400 million yuan, currently stored in the vaults of Federal Reserve Banks, may be exported one after another.

New Japanese Budget 98

Breaks 2.3 Billion

Tokyo, 19th (Dentsu) – The budget for Showa 8 (1933) has reached 2,239 million yen due to the need to spend on urgent Manchurian Incident expenses, military preparation expenses, and situation relief expenses. This is an unprecedentedly huge amount in Japanese financial history. Afterwards, 64 million yen for Manchurian Incident relief funds, Hokkaido disaster relief expenses, naval factory capital replenishment funds, and other temporary necessities were proposed in the supplementary budget. Therefore, the total budget for general accounting is 2,303 million yen, which has been passed by the House of Representatives and will also be passed by the House of Peers within two or three days. However, due to the necessity of emergency measures for the Great Sanriku Earthquake, it is difficult to spend from the reserve fund. Therefore, the Ministry of Interior, the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, and other related ministries have requested 10 million yen. However, it is difficult to approve the full amount due to the limited time remaining in the session. As a result, half of the amount, 5 million yen, will be approved. If so, the total budget for general accounting for Showa 8 will reach 2,310 million yen.

The Deadly Enemy of Japanese Militarists 100

Dr. Yoshino Passes Away

Tokyo, 19th (Hua-Ren) – Dr. Sakuzo Yoshino, advisor to the Social Mass Party and Doctor of Law, died in Zushi last night at the age of 56. He was born in Miyagi Prefecture in 1878. He graduated from the Faculty of Law of Tokyo Imperial University in 1904 and immediately went to study political science in various European countries. After returning to China, he served as a professor at Tokyo Imperial University. At the end of the European War, he advocated democracy, rejected militarist autocracy, and strongly condemned the military for abusing its power to destroy democracy and engaging in rampant dual diplomacy. He recently became an opponent of the military, which soon led to his dismissal from his teaching position at Tokyo Imperial University. He then served as an advisor to the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun, and was again forced to leave by the military due to his essay causing a disrespect charge. Afterwards, he served as a lecturer at Waseda University and as an advisor to the Social Mass Party until his death, being an enemy of Japanese militarists.
