Public Telegram 102

Telegram from Zhou – To all newspaper offices, transferred to philanthropists at home and abroad, be advised that the counties of Huangchuan, Guangshan, Shangcheng, Fuli, Huang, and Tongshi in Henan have long suffered from banditry and disaster. The countryside has become a scorched earth, and the refugees after the robbery relied on tree bark and grass roots to barely survive. Although they have repeatedly received generous relief from the government and domestic philanthropists, it is like a drop in the bucket, difficult to be universal. Recently, the spring cold has been unusually severe, and new grass has not yet grown. The need to fill their bellies has become hopeless. Some hang themselves, others starve to death on the roads, and the corpses are piled up in the fields, which is unbearable to see. Even the living are emaciated and difficult to survive. If relief is not urgently provided, I am afraid that they will take risks and the ashes will rekindle. This will not only abandon the achievements of suppressing the bandits, but also affect the overall situation. As the successor to supervising Yuzhong, I witness this with a heavy heart and implore all charitable organizations, kind people, and benevolent people to generously issue compassionate hearts, quickly issue large amounts of relief funds, and allocate grain in batches to urgently relieve and save the hundreds of thousands of refugees in southern Henan who are about to die. I earnestly plead, with endless anticipation. Chen Jicheng, Commander of the First Army and Administrative Supervisor of the Ninth District of Henan, respectfully knocks.

The Formation of the New Fascist Cabinet in Germany 103

(German Correspondence) Huang Gongan

New Figures in the New Cabinet

Under the instructions of President Hindenburg, Germany once again produced a new cabinet yesterday (Sunday, January 30, 1933). Hitler, the leader of the National Socialist Labor Party, also known as the German Fascist Party, was appointed as the new Prime Minister. Papen, the former Prime Minister who had resigned twice, also made a comeback and was appointed as the Deputy Prime Minister and Special Commissioner of the Prussian State Government. The remaining cabinet members were assigned as follows:

Foreign Minister: Neurath

Interior Minister: Dr. Frick

Defense Minister: General Blomberg

Finance Minister: Count Schwerin von Krosigk

Minister of Economics, Food and Agriculture: Dr. Hugenberg

Labor Minister: Seldte

Minister of Postal Services and Transport: Eltz von Rübenach

Aviation Minister: Göring

Justice Minister: (Undecided)

With the exception of Foreign Minister Neurath, who is a member of the previous cabinet, all the other members of the new cabinet are newcomers to the political stage and are all extremely right-wing figures who came from the Fascist Nationalistic movement. Left-wing parties such as the Social Democratic Party and the Communist Party, as well as the moderate Central Party, were excluded, or refused to cooperate with the right-wing, and had no representatives participating in this cabinet formation. The Social Democratic Party's Forward Daily criticized the cabinet members from a social perspective, saying that they all represent the reactionary forces of big capitalists, big industrialists, big landlords, feudal ideology, and the Fascist united front. In addition, from the perspective of general public opinion, it is generally recognized that the new cabinet is a three-headed cabinet of Hitler, Papen, and Hugenberg. This party is a neutral, objective, and unbiased argument.

The Process of Forming the New Cabinet 104

The process of forming the new cabinet in Germany was very simple and took less time than usual. President Hindenburg also used political skills to swiftly and resolutely approve the resignation of the Schleicher cabinet and immediately decide to call Hitler to form a cabinet. This was a remarkable achievement. The process of this cabinet change did not cause any political unrest or any major social disturbances. It went smoothly, which is a rare phenomenon in German cabinet changes. Former Prime Minister Schleicher resigned in late January because the new Parliament could not form a majority government, which caused resentment and disappointment among government officials. In addition, the two extreme parties on the left and right in Parliament did not trust or sympathize with Schleicher. On the other hand, since Schleicher took office as Prime Minister, his various policies to address economic panic and unemployment were too passive, and his own political direction was not clearly expressed. The cabinet was in a passive political position, which led to the loss of strong social support and sympathy from political parties. He fought alone and could not hold on, and as a result, he was at a loss. Moreover, the so-called Eastern Aid Plan (a plan to help farmers in East Prussia) lacked a fully satisfactory and active effective design, which especially dissatisfied East Prussian landlords and farmers, leading to attacks on Schleicher and a movement to overthrow the cabinet. In addition, it was heard that Schleicher and Hindenburg's son had disagreements. The environment was bad and he was surrounded by enemies, which made it extremely difficult for the Schleicher cabinet to act. Finally, because Schleicher's proposal to Hindenburg to dissolve the Parliament again was not approved, his policies became increasingly unsuccessful, and he had to submit the cabinet's collective resignation to Hindenburg on January 29. After receiving Schleicher's letter of resignation, Hindenburg, given the Schleicher cabinet's inability to do anything, certainly could not let him stay for a long time and miss the opportunity. Hindenburg immediately approved the resignation. From then on, Schleicher's term as Prime Minister lasted only 75 days. After this cabinet change, the Fascist Party, which had been lurking for a long time, took this opportunity to make a big publicity campaign, unanimously supporting Fascist leader Hitler to take office. At this time, Hindenburg, looking around at the domestic situation, had no other talent in mind to succeed the cabinet other than Hitler. Although Hindenburg clearly knew that Hitler had once competed with him for the presidency and competed with each other, and in fact was a political enemy, it seemed impossible to cooperate or obey. However, President Hindenburg witnessed that the economic panic and suffering were becoming increasingly serious, the unemployment problem was becoming increasingly severe and worsening, and the calls and realities of the left-leaning proletariat revolution were like a raging wind and advancing day by day. Externally, there were issues such as striving for equal international status, war debts, and the constraints of the Treaty of Versailles. The Fascist Party has been making the greatest efforts for this kind of domestic and foreign liberation movement in recent years. Therefore, for the sake of strengthening the entire country and seeking the welfare of the entire nation, Hindenburg had to abandon his past grievances, change his strategy, and establish confidence in good faith. He was willing to work with Hitler to jointly solve Germany's current tense political situation. First, Hindenburg ordered former Prime Minister Papen to come forward and negotiate with right-wing leaders such as Hitler. At that time, Hindenburg also proposed the following cooperation conditions:

(1) Request Hitler to serve as Prime Minister, but on the premise that he abandon his previous advocacy of personal dictatorship.

(2) Require the organization of a national government, broadly including cooperation with the leader of the German National People's Party, Hugenberg, and Papen.

(3) In the future, cabinet policies should abandon the various new economic system experiments of the Fascist Party and implement various new policies under the conditions that they are in line with the wishes of the majority of the people of the country and do not violate the spirit and principles of the Weimar Constitution.

Hitler expressed understanding and willingness to accept these negotiation conditions. As a result, Hitler was appointed as the new Prime Minister on January 30, marking the beginning of a purely right-leaning trend in German politics. At the same time, it also marked the first time the German Fascist Party had set foot on the glorious stage of German politics. Therefore, Hitler's patriotic movement, which he had been running around and calling for for fourteen years, had gone through many hardships, and was difficult to build, and his political ambition can be said to have reached the first step of its goal. Now Hitler can actually show his political skills.

Reflections on Public Opinion at Home and Abroad 0 105

(1) Influence of Domestic Public Opinion

Since the formal public announcement of the Hindenburg's new three-headed cabinet, it goes without saying that all political parties and newspapers standing on the right-wing front naturally expressed extreme joy and satisfaction, congratulating the right-wing politics for gaining power. Especially the members of the German Fascist Party, since their leader was appointed to the new cabinet, were overjoyed and ecstatic. Members across the country immediately convened extraordinary conferences to celebrate and march, with party members all wearing military uniforms, rampaging through the squares and avenues, their faces filled with seemingly boundless glory. They immediately sent telegrams expressing unanimous support for the new cabinet, vowing that the twelve million Fascist Party members would be Hindenburg's cabinet's rear guard.

But from the left-wing perspective, such as the Democratic Party, the Iron Front, the Free Trade Union, and the Communist Party, the emergence of this three-headed cabinet is seen as the epitome of politics dominated by big capitalists, big landlords, feudal remnants, gentry classes, warlords, militarists, and Fascist dictatorship. In short, it is the great success of the united reactionary forces holding the right-wing (front). This reactionary group has always opposed the interests of workers, promoted capitalism, advocated imperialist policies, practiced dictatorship, undermined democracy, and violated the constitution. Now that they have suddenly leaped onto the political stage and manipulated national power, they will inevitably pose an unfavorable threat or a fatal oppression to the left wing. Therefore, for the sake of maintaining their own survival and the interests of the working class and proletariat, the left-wing front has no choice but to unanimously, resolutely, and actively express opposition to the Hindenburg's new cabinet. The Communist Party's newspaper "Red Flag" and the Social Democratic Party's newspaper "Forward" immediately published fierce and powerful declarations attacking the new cabinet, and demanded that workers on the left-wing front hold a national general strike to give the new government and Hindenburg a serious warning with practical actions, and so on. Newspapers standing completely neutral generally believe that the emergence of this new cabinet is the best symbol of coordination between Hindenburg and Hitler, and at the same time, the ultimate success of right-wing compromise, cooperation, and sincere unity in jointly resisting the left-leaning forces. The people, standing on a non-partisan position and taking the overall welfare of the nation as a premise, weighing this new cabinet, can indeed regard it as a fortunate event. We can find this kind of opinion in the "German Gazette." However, the Center Party is unwilling to participate in cooperation with Hindenburg's cabinet and does not express opposition, maintaining a policy of tolerance. Hindenburg once offered the position of Minister of Justice to a member of the Center Party, but the Center Party refused to accept it. The attitude is detached, with a sense of "I am sober while everyone else is drunk," which is really difficult to understand. It is unknown what they are up to.

(2) Repercussions of Foreign Public Opinion

After the emergence of Hindenburg's new cabinet in Germany, the most meaningful impact abroad was in Rome. After receiving the news that Hitler had come to power in Germany and formed a cabinet, Rome believed that the emergence of another Fascist dictatorship comrade in a neighboring country brought immense comfort to Mussolini. All Italian public opinion expressed goodwill towards the new German government. However, France's perception was exactly the opposite of Italy's. After receiving the special telegram that Hitler had come to power in Germany and formed a cabinet, the right-wing newspapers in Paris felt dizzy and bewildered, suffering a great blow and a dangerous threat to their spirits. Although Hitler did not launch a revenge challenge against France, France already felt the seriousness of the security issue. As a result, the right-wing elements in France once again strongly demanded that the government increase the defense budget, and the relations between Germany and France suddenly became very tense again. The Moscow government's unwillingness for the German right wing to be in power was the same as France's, because Fascist nationalism and Slavic internationalism are fundamentally incompatible. Moscow knows that the activities of German Communist Party comrades will not be banned or restricted in the future, so it expresses deep dissatisfaction. In recent years, Britain and the United States have become slightly closer to Germany. There is little discrimination and no dangerous suspicion between each other internationally. Therefore, no matter how German politics changes, it will not have a major direct impact on Britain and the United States. Therefore, the criticism and observation of the emergence of the new German cabinet in London and New York this time is very objective. It is neither as bewildered as France nor as hostile as Soviet Russia. The only greatest and most urgent hope of Britain and the United States is that Germany itself can truly unite, curb the intensification of left-leaning tendencies, and quickly seek to solve the economic panic and restore the normality of international trade, so that Britain and the United States can also suffer less from the world economic panic, so they are very happy about it. Swiss public opinion is also the same as the aforementioned countries, all with a special and unique perspective. For example, the two major Swiss newspapers believe that Hitler's rise to power is the best symbol of the rise of Fascist dictatorship in Germany and the demise of parliamentary democracy (To be continued)

Situation in North China After Zhang Xueliang's Resignation 106

A special dispatch from Peiping states that after the fall of Chengde, the situation in North China suddenly became tense. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek came north to take charge in order to develop military and diplomatic affairs. He met with Zhang in Baoding, and with Yan in Shijiazhuang, to jointly plan major strategies. He also sent Li Liejun to urge Feng to go to Baoding to discuss everything in person. Because of the change in the situation, Zhang had to resolutely resign to make way for the more capable. After leaving Peiping, the northern situation will be temporarily presided over by He Yingqin, who will serve as the Minister of Military Administration and concurrently as the Chairman of the Peiping Branch of the Military Affairs Commission. After He took office, important officials of the Military Affairs Commission, such as Rong Zhen, Wan Fulin, Zhu Guangmu, and Tang Guozhen, resigned one after another. He earnestly retained them all. Except for Zhu and Tang, who left with Zhang and could not be retained, the rest were not changed. Even the lower-level personnel remained as they were, without any reduction or additional appointments. This is because, in the current situation, it is only possible to temporarily maintain the status quo and it is not convenient to make any changes. Yesterday, He ordered the adjutant's office to notify all subordinates to address him as Minister He, and not to honor him as Chairman. From this, He's intentions can be seen.

Since Zhang's resignation, many military and political personnel under the Northeast system have shown their intention to leave. Letters and telegrams of resignation have been coming one after another. Military leaders such as Wan Fulin, Wang Shuchang, Rong Zhen, Wang Yizhe, Shen Honglie, and Bao Yulin have all resigned once. Important political figures such as Zhou Dawen have also expressed their intention to leave. Chiang Kai-shek and He Yingqin have been urging them to work together to overcome the difficulties during this national crisis. In addition to Chiang Kai-shek and Zhang Xueliang agreeing in Baoding to reorganize the Northeast Army into four armies, with each taking on the positions of the 1st, 2nd, 3rd, and 4th Army Commanders, the rest are earnestly retained and will never be transferred. The previously determined Commander of the Peiping-Tianjin Garrison, Xu Tingyao, and the Mayor of Peiping, Huang Fu, have been implicitly dismissed. The Northeast military and political personnel believe that although Zhang has resigned, someone is still in charge, and during this difficult time, they should also put the country first and continue to work hard, and wait until this difficult period is over before making further plans. Chiang Kai-shek's meeting in Shijiazhuang was fruitful. It was agreed that the defense and security of the Chahar border would be the responsibility of the Jin-Sui army. It is said that the troops of Fu Zuoyi and Wang Jingguo have entered Chahar Province and the defense is consolidated. It was originally intended to transfer Fu Zuoyi, the Chairman of Suiyuan Province, to Chahar Province, and Wang Jingguo to Suiyuan. However, recently, due to the imminent foreign invasion and the urgency of national salvation, it is not appropriate to make too many internal changes to avoid reducing the external forces. This proposal had to be temporarily shelved. Chiang Kai-shek hopes that Feng Yuxiang can come to Baoding for a talk to discuss major strategies. Li Liejun was ordered to go to Zhangjiakou to meet Feng Yuxiang and convey Chiang Kai-shek's intentions, urging him to go south quickly. However, Feng Yuxiang responded to Chiang Kai-shek's sincere invitation with ambiguous answers, and has not yet prepared to leave Zhangjiakou, probably unwilling to leave Chahar Province easily in order to implement his recent anti-Japanese proposals and is willing to fight the enemy on the front line.

As for diplomacy, since Luo Wengan went north and shuttled between Peiping and Baoding, and consulted with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and the ambassadors of various countries, a new development has taken place. The security in the customs may be temporarily maintained. After the Japanese army occupied Rehe, it takes time to deploy, and there is no force to advance south for a while. Recently, it suffered a major setback outside Xifengkou, and its momentum has been reduced. Although the Japanese army still has the determination to obtain it, it has no ability to fight fiercely without new reinforcements. Recently, the Gubeikou area has entered a state of truce. It is said that Mutō has already entered Rehe, with the purpose of preventing the Japanese army from advancing and temporarily taking the Great Wall area as its line of defense. If this is true, the two sides may temporarily form a confrontational situation in the future. (March 17)

Officers and Soldiers of Su, Li, and Others 107

Arrive in Peiping

Totaling One Thousand Five Hundred and Four People

Returning from Russia via Vladivostok

Peiping News: The officers, soldiers, dependents, and refugees of the troops of Su Bingwen, Li Du, Wang Delin, etc., who had retreated into Russian territory with Su, etc., returned to China by ship via Vladivostok. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Peiping at 6:00 pm on the 16th, but due to delays along the way, it did not arrive at the East Station until 11:10 pm that night. At about 8:00 pm, representatives from all walks of life went to the station to welcome them, including the representatives of the Liaoning-Jilin-Heilongjiang Support Association, Guo Erjia, Zhao Zhongqi, Ma Zhanshan's representative, Duan Zhongfan, Su Bingwen's representative, Fan Ruizheng, Su's son, Su Zongjun, Li Du's representative, Du Hongnian, Wang Delin's representative, Li Bingyi, and the Red Cross representative, Tang Hengyuan, the Northeast Refugee Relief Institute representative, Zhang Wenhui, and the Buddhist Association representative, Zeng Guangshan, etc. The Liaoning-Jilin-Heilongjiang Support Association had also prepared ten cars, the Public Security Bureau five cars, and the Red Cross one car to meet them at the station in advance. After 10:30, some representatives from all walks of life returned early due to martial law. At 11:05, the special train arrived at the station, and the dependents and refugee representatives got off the train and greeted the welcomers, which was quite busy. According to a representative, Su Bingwen's subordinates took the Siberian train from Omsk to Vladivostok, and Su's wife and daughter transferred to Europe. Wang Delin's subordinates and Li Du's subordinates took the China Eastern Railway from Hulin County on the west bank of the Ussuri River to Vladivostok. They took a ship to Tanggu on the 9th, and took a car from Tanggu to Peiping. Wang Delin's wife led 136 of his subordinates to Shanghai by ship. A total of 1,504 people came together, including 1,260 from Su's troops, 46 from Li's troops, and 188 from Wang's troops. Among them, 796 were women and 708 were men (including 19 wounded soldiers). The general representatives of the people were Ren Zuotian, Zhang Datong, Guo Zhutang, and Yang Dafang. In addition to the families of various officers, there were also lower-level officers and soldiers and refugees. Li Du's wife also arrived in Peiping, etc. The Liaoning-Jilin-Heilongjiang Support Association is responsible for the reception. The order of getting off the train and sending them was: first the wounded soldiers, then the women, and finally the men. They will all be accommodated in the New World. If that place cannot accommodate them, they will be accommodated in the Xisi Diwang Temple and the Northeast Refugee Relief Institute. It was not until after 1:00 that the transportation was completed. Also, when the train arrived in Tianjin, Zhang Xueming sent 1,200 towels and soaps. Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong also sent representatives to the station to express condolences. (March 17)

Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's 108

Office in Jiangxi Moves to Baoding

Led by Qian Dajun Heading North

Responsible for Suppression of Communists in Southwest

A dispatch from Nanchang states that after Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went north the other day, he telegraphed Qian Dajun, the director of the Military Affairs Commission's office in Jiangxi, to lead all the staff of the office north to assist in military operations, as the anti-Japanese military situation is tense. After receiving the order, Qian left Jiangxi on the 15th with the confidential secretary Deng Wenyi, the confidential staff officers, secretaries, adjutants, and personnel from various departments and went to Baoding. All unfinished matters of the headquarters and the military affairs of suppressing bandits in the province were handled by the Jiangxi-Guangdong-Fujian Border Area Bandit Suppression Headquarters, which was headed by Chief of Staff He Guang on an acting basis. The front line was the responsibility of Chen Cheng, the commander-in-chief of the central route. However, when Chiang first came to Jiangxi, the southwest had expressed the hope that Chiang would go north to resist Japan and the southwest would be responsible for suppressing the Communists. Now that Chiang has gone north to supervise the troops, the southwest should fulfill its previous statement. It is said that Chiang's military affairs of suppressing the Communists in the three provinces will be presided over by Chen Jitang. Chen's representative, Li Shangyong, arrived in the province yesterday, and there will be important contacts and discussions on the progress of suppressing the Communists. (March 17)

Jiangxi Troops Recover Jianning 109

Fujian and Jiangxi Troops Jointly Suppress Communist Bandits in Border Area

Provincial Government Exempts Taxes in Recovered Bandit Areas

A dispatch from Fuzhou states that after the Fujian and Jiangxi troops jointly attacked Jianning and Guangchang, the Guangchang Red Bandits have collapsed and retreated towards Shicheng. The Jianning Red Bandits have also retreated towards Ninghua under its influence. The Jiangxi troops then sent Guo Siyuan's division to pursue from Guangchang to Shicheng, and another division, Zhao Guantao's 6th Division, advanced from Nanfeng towards Jianning, and occupied Jianning County on the 11th. Currently, most of the Red Bandits on the Fujian-Jiangxi border have gathered between the four counties of Ninghua, Changting, Shicheng, and Ruijin, and are building fortifications to resist. Cai Tingkai has transferred Lu Xingbang's division's two brigades, Lu Xingrong and Zhang Xinglong, from Qingliu to advance, Zhang Yan's division's two brigades, Pang Chengyun and Lin, from Liancheng to advance, and Huang Renhuan's division's two brigades, Yan Yingyu and Zeng Youren, from Shanghang to advance, in three routes to attack Ninghua and Changting. At the same time, the Jiangxi troops also sent about five divisions of troops to surround Shicheng and Ruijin to take a pincer attack. Currently, all Fujian troops have reached the front line. In addition, Zhang Zhen's division is stationed in Yongding, Shen Guanghan's division is stationed in Longyan, Qu Shounian's division is stationed in Zhangping, Liu Heding's division is stationed in Tai Ning, Zhou Zhijun's brigade is stationed in Guangze, Qian Yuguang's brigade is stationed in Jian'ou, and Zhang Luanji's brigade is stationed in Pucheng, to take charge of the rear defense of western and northern Fujian, and to support the front line, waiting for the Jiangxi troops to launch a full-scale general attack. However, according to military news, a part of the Red Bandits in Lichuan sneaked into Guangze and Tai Ning again on the 13th, looting wantonly. On the 15th, they had a battle with Zhou Zhijun's and Liu Hezhong's troops, and the artillery fire was quite fierce. Also, the Chong'an Red Bandits and Zhang Luanji's and Qian Yuguang's troops are confronting each other between Chishi in the eastern district and Lan Gu in the western district. As for the provincial government, as the military affairs of suppressing bandits have been progressing rapidly recently, the areas occupied by the bandits have been recovered one after another, and it is urgent to carry out post-war reconstruction to stabilize the people's livelihood. In addition to sending the refugees from the bandit areas who have been wandering in various places back to their hometowns to engage in farming during this spring, the provincial government meeting on the 15th decided to exempt all the old debts and this year's Ding and Zao taxes that should be paid in the recently recovered bandit areas to show sympathy. The administrative expenses of the local government will also be subsidized by the provincial treasury to alleviate the burden. (March 16)

Hankou Headquarters 110

Plans to Establish Four Provinces Farmers Bank

Total Capital of Ten Million Yuan

Purpose: To Revive the Rural Economy

A dispatch from Hankou states that the Commander-in-Chief of the Bandit Suppression Headquarters in the four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi believes that the farmers in the bandit areas of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi are in extremely difficult situations after the recovery, and it is necessary to find ways to provide relief in order to recover. In order to provide farmers with funds, revive the rural economy, and promote the improvement and progress of agricultural production, the establishment of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui-Jiangxi Farmers Bank is specially permitted, and Guo Waifeng, the director of the Rural Financial Relief Office, is concurrently appointed as the preparatory director. Preparations have been completed and it will be established soon. The regulations of the bank have been formulated by the headquarters and will be promulgated and implemented on the 18th, and will be ordered to the provincial governments of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi to comply with them and sent to the Executive Yuan for record. The original text of the regulations is about 2,000 words. The main points are: (1) The total capital is set at 10 million yuan in national currency, and business can be started when one-quarter is paid up. The fundraising methods are: 1. 3 million yuan invested by the national treasury, 2. 500,000 yuan invested by the provincial treasuries of the four provinces, and 3. 5 million yuan raised from commercial shares. (2) The head office is located in Hankou, and branches and offices will be established within the four provinces as appropriate. The business period is set at 60 years. (3) The scope of business includes: 1. Mortgage loans for movable and immovable property, and guaranteed credit loans, 2. Discounting and rediscounting of agricultural notes, 3. Accepting various deposits, 4. Acting as an agent for receiving and remitting various funds, 5. Handling remittances and short-term transactions with the same industry, 6. Buying and selling raw gold and silver and valuable securities issued by the National Government, 7. Operating agricultural warehouses and lending to the improvement of agricultural products and agricultural implements, 8. Lending to cooperative societies and federations of cooperative societies at all levels organized by farmers, 9. Issuing agricultural bonds and farmer circulation coupons, 10. Other businesses that a farmers bank should have. (4) The uses of the loans are: 1. Purchasing plowing cattle, seeds, fertilizers, livestock, and various agricultural raw materials, 2. Purchasing or repairing agricultural machinery, 3. Transportation and storage of agricultural products, 4. Constructing agricultural buildings and yards, 5. Other matters closely related to agriculture that are considered necessary, using fixed-term repayment or installment repayment methods, for a maximum period of no more than five years. (5) The organization consists of a board of directors composed of nine directors, with three standing directors, whose duties are: 1. Reviewing the business policy, 2. Compiling the articles of association and various rules and regulations of the head and branch offices, 3. Nominating the general manager and assistant manager, 4. Issuing agricultural bonds and farmer circulation coupons, 5. Reviewing the budget and final accounts, 6. Deciding on capital increases and decreases, 7. Other suggestions. There are four supervisors, whose duties are: 1. Checking cash, 2. Auditing accounts, 3. Auditing the budget and final accounts, 4. Other family matters. There is one general manager and one assistant manager, who manage and assist in handling the affairs of the entire bank. Each branch has one manager, and may add an assistant manager when necessary. (6) The final accounts are to be made in December of each year as the general accounting period, and reports are prepared separately. The directors and supervisors should be elected by the shareholders meeting. Before the commercial shares are fully subscribed to half, the shareholders meeting will not be convened temporarily, and will be selected and appointed by the headquarters. The standing directors will also be appointed by the headquarters, and the general manager will be nominated by the board of directors and submitted to the headquarters for appointment. All the powers stipulated in the regulations to be exercised by the headquarters will be transferred to the central competent authorities after the headquarters is abolished. (March 18)

Songjiang 111

Tenant Farmer Angrily Commits Suicide by Cutting His Throat in the Granary

Dong Yuyu, a resident west of Malu Bridge in this city, had farmland in Qingpu rented to a farmer named Wang Heshang who lived in Shatianbang outside the north gate of Qingpu. Wang Heshang was supposed to pay more than eleven stone of rent. The seeds had already been sent to the granary by Wang Heshang early on. After returning home, he was blamed by his children and daughters-in-law for paying too much and urged him to go to Songjiang to calculate and get it back. Wang Heshang, who was over sixty years old, was filled with anger. Yesterday (the 18th) he came to Songjiang to settle accounts with Dong's granary. The owner of the granary replied that he had not calculated too much and refused his request. The farmer was unable to return home, so he borrowed lodging there. At noon today, he borrowed five hundred cash from Dong, pretending to buy snacks to fill his stomach. He returned after a while and said he was dizzy. He went upstairs to take a nap, but secretly used a pointed foot knife to cut his throat on the right side. Blood flowed all over the bed. When someone noticed, it was too late to save him, and he died. It was about 2:00 pm. The knife used for suicide was probably the one he borrowed money to buy outside. After the incident, the Public Security Bureau and the Procuratorate of the Court were notified to request an inspection, and people were sent to the village to report to his family.

Fundraising for Aircraft Donation - Mass Propaganda 112

Since the organization of the Aircraft Donation Fundraising Committee from all walks of life, donations have not been enthusiastic. It was decided to hold a mass propaganda campaign at the auditorium of the People's Education Hall at 1:00 pm today (the 19th). Representatives from various agencies and the entire student body of the school attended, and the public also participated enthusiastically. After the chairman of the county party committee led the ceremony, he gave a speech on the importance of the air force as a weapon to defeat the enemy. If we want to resist the stubborn enemy, the public should donate money to purchase aircraft to alleviate the national crisis. After the meeting, there were also performances, including Pingtan by the Datong Theater, songs and dances by the school, and martial arts performances at the sports field to help promote the campaign.

Wuxi 113

Primary School Students Enthusiastically Patriotic

The sixth elementary school of Shishangwan County in the northern countryside of this county has more than 360 students. Recently, due to the rampant behavior of the Japanese invaders and the deepening national crisis, they have been saving money on candy and donating to the national salvation fund for aviation. Senior students donate four corners of a dollar per person, and junior students donate two corners of a dollar per person. Together with the savings of the school teachers, the amount is considerable.

Three People Burned to Death in a Fire in Xiaosi Alley 114

In the vicinity of Xiaosi Alley outside the north gate of this county, Cai Yuxing's steamer shop, which was opened by Cai Kaiyu, and the landlord Qian Zixuan, whose family runs a paper horse business, had a total of three buildings. The tenants Pan Achun (who opened Pan Wanxing's bamboo basket shop), Zhu Xueming (who opened Zhu Yishun's gluten shop), Zhu Yubao (who opened Zhu Hengtai's foreign goods shop), and Wang Jin's and Wang Ating's mother and son, a total of fifteen or sixteen men and women, all lived upstairs and downstairs. Yesterday morning (the 19th) at about 2:00, a fire suddenly broke out in the building, causing a fire. The fire immediately broke through the roof. Zhu Yubao's wife, Leng, their son Lingzhu, and Wang Jin's son, Ating, were burned to death because they could not escape. The fire brigades of each section heard the alarm and drove dragons to the scene, drawing water to extinguish the fire. It took two hours to put out the fire. A total of three buildings in the back were burned down. The burned corpses have been dug out of the rubble, charred and unrecognizable.

Changshu 115

Robbery Case in Xiaochuan Bay

In the Xiaochuan Bay area near Dahe Town in the ninth district, there is a farmer named Cai Yongjia who is quite wealthy. Fearing that he would be coveted by bandits, he dug a cave underground to hide his silver, hoping to be discreet. Unexpectedly, three robbers armed with kitchen knives and iron rulers came to Cai's house to rob him the night before. They tied up Yongjia, used a hook to hook his nostrils, and forced him to ask where the silver was hidden. Although Cai firmly refused to reveal it, he was eventually searched and more than 2,000 yuan were robbed.

Yangzhou 116

More News of the Massacre on a Civilian Boat

Inside the Shaobo Zhaoguan Dam Canal, on the morning of the 17th, an empty civilian boat with no one on board was discovered. A case of four people being brutally murdered was found on the boat. Yang Guoxiang, the head of the eighth district of Shaobo, went to investigate. The boat was parked in front of the Bamboo Forest Temple. There were two male corpses in the front cabin, both without shirts, about forty years old. There was a female corpse next to the helm, also about forty years old, with several axe wounds on her head, face, and arms. Next to the female corpse was a four-year-old boy with sixteen axe wounds on his head and neck and bruises on his body. In the front cabin were a bloody axe, two soft-brimmed gray military caps. Eight boat registration documents were found in the rear cabin, one with the words "boat owner Li Zhongliang" and one with the words "Siyang Civilian Boat Trade Association member Li Yutian." There was also a business card with the words "Chen Zhencai, also known as Yu Zeng, standing committee member of the Yangjing Port Boat Workers Union in Shanghai Special Municipality." There was also an envelope from the union addressed to Wang Zhong's drugstore in Qian Dajie, Xuyi County, Anhui Province, to be forwarded to Li Yutian. After Yang inspected the area, he reported it to the county government and sent a letter to the Jiangdu Local Branch of the court requesting officials to come and inspect.

Nantong 117

Tax Police Captain Abducted and Killed

Kuang Yexiong, the captain of the fourth district tax police stationed in Tongzhou, under the Ministry of Finance's Supervisory Tax Police, led a team to Dongxiang to patrol for smuggled salt. He encountered a large group of outlaws in Yiyu and was abducted. After being severely beaten, he was torn apart and killed. In addition to ordering the county to hunt down the murderers, the Ministry of Finance decided to hold a memorial service at the Xisi Temple in Nantong on the 25th, gathering the tax police officers stationed in the counties of Tongzhou, Rugao, Taixing, and Hai'an.

Wang Ren Transferred to Shanghai Special District Court 118

Wang Ren, a prosecutor at the Nantong County Court, was ordered by the Ministry of Judicial Administration to be transferred to the Shanghai Special District Court as a judge. His vacancy will be filled by Meng Tingke, a judge from the Jiangning District Court.

Hefei 119

Four Zhen District Smashes Gun-Making Organization

According to a report from Rong Xian, the commander of the Second Security Regiment, there were Xie Bangcun and others who privately set up a gun factory in the Four Zhen District of the northeast to manufacture and transport weapons and ammunition to help bandits. He secretly sent a team to the address and seized many guns and ammunition, and arrested seven officials, including Xie Banglu, gunsmiths Qu Xiny, Hua Shanlu, and Wang Guozhi, and sent them to the county for questioning.

Wang Jingwei and Song Ziwen Went to the Capital Together Last Night 120

Wang Still Hopes Song Will Truly Take Office

Song Determined to Return to Shanghai in a Few Days

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, and Song Ziwen, the Acting President of the Yuan, took the overnight express train with an attached special carriage to the capital last night at 11:30. Details are as follows:

Tight Security 121

Wen Hongen, the director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, personally led more than ten armed policemen and fifty members of the security team last night to maintain strict security on the main roads in and out of the North Station and in front of and behind President Wang's special carriage.

Wang and Song in the Same Car 122

At 11:15 AM, President Wang, along with his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Tie Ci, Zeng Zhongming, arrived at the station and immediately boarded the PC502 limousine. President Song arrived at the North Station at 11:25 AM with his secretary, Huang Chun, and joined President Wang in the same car. They departed at 11:30 AM.

Wang's Remarks 123

President Wang told reporters that the position of President of the Executive Yuan involves numerous affairs and heavy responsibilities. Due to his incomplete recovery, he is unable to handle the workload. Forcing himself to take on the role might lead to incompetence and harm the country. Although various parties have strongly urged him to resume his duties, he still maintains his previous stance and hopes that President Song will be officially appointed. As for whether or not he will go north, he will decide after arriving in Beijing.

Chiang to Come to Beijing Soon 124

According to sources close to Wang, Chairman Chiang of the Military Affairs Commission, will arrive in Beijing by plane from Baoding after Wang arrives, to meet and discuss important issues such as the war of resistance against Japan, military affairs, and diplomacy. Regarding the matter of Wang's resumption of the presidency of the Executive Yuan, Wang has been persuaded by various parties in Shanghai for days, and his intentions have already been swayed. It is likely that a final decision will be made after meeting with Chiang.

Song's Determination 125

It is said that President Song's telegram to Beijing resigning from his acting position shows extreme determination. He has scheduled the Executive Yuan meeting for the 21st and intends to return to Shanghai before the 21st after meeting with Chiang in Beijing, to express his resolve to relinquish his responsibilities.

Traveling Companions 126

Those who traveled to Beijing with President Wang and President Song last night included Minister of Industry Chen Gongbo, Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua, Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Shi Qingyang, Tie Ci Zeng Zhongming, Secretary-General of the Central Political Committee Tang Youren, Secretary-General of the Executive Yuan Chu Minyi, Vice Minister Gan Naiguang, Secretary-General of the Legislative Yuan Liang Han Cao, Vice Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission Bai Yunti, Vice Minister Zou Lin, and Chief of Staff of the National Government Lu Chao, among others. Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu is scheduled to take the express train to Beijing this morning.

Fierce Battles Imminent on the Front Lines 127

Enemy Defeated at Xifengkou Reinforced

Our Troops on High Alert

People Urged to Quickly Raise Relief Funds

Zhu Qinglan's Urgent Telegram: The Shanghai Northeast Relief Association received a telegram from Zhu Ziqiao stating, "Gentlemen of all associations, after the enemy's disastrous defeat at Xifengkou, they have been bombing our positions with large numbers of aircraft for days to contain us. Meanwhile, they have been rapidly advancing and fiercely attacking our Luowenyu positions with a mixed brigade or more of troops, attempting to disrupt our rear. Commander Liu Ruming of Song's division led three regiments to counterattack, resulting in a fierce battle lasting all day and night. The enemy concentrated its firepower with artillery and planes, bombing our army with dozens of aircraft, but our troops remained steadfast. Subsequently, Commander Liu, with bare arms and holding a saber, led his troops to charge the enemy, killing four to five hundred men, breaking through two lines of enemy defenses, capturing enemy officers and soldiers, and seizing many guns, cannons, and bullets. A small number of the enemy fled, and the majority were annihilated. They are now increasing reinforcements, aiming to capture Xifengkou, and a fierce battle is imminent. The front lines lack supplies, and the bloody battles are almost without resources. The casualties among officers and soldiers also await relief. Thinking of this, I cannot help but feel extremely saddened. Your patriotic hearts are undoubtedly even more fervent than mine. I implore you to quickly raise substantial funds, gather a large quantity of medicine, and transport them quickly to the front lines to meet the urgent needs. This is my sincere hope." Zhu Qinglan bows urgently.

Sun Dianying's Urgent Telegram: The Northeast Refugee Relief Association, the Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association, and the Shanghai Northeast Refugee Relief Association received a telegram dated the 16th from Sun Kuiyuan stating, "I have just received a telegram from our army's office in Peiping, and I thank you for the consolation money of ten thousand yuan. At this time of national crisis and financial hardship, our army is defending the country, which is our duty. Your comrades have gathered contributions, showing deep patriotism, and I am deeply grateful for your generous assistance. In the future, we will continue to strive to live up to your kindness. We will notify you separately upon receipt of the funds. I respectfully wish you all the best. Sun Kuiyuan, Commander of the Forty-first Army, bows. Sun also telegraphed Zhang Youqun, his representative in Shanghai, saying, 'Brother Youqun, I have received your telegram. Our army has been fighting hard for over ten days, and we are in dire straits. Not only are we running out of ammunition, but we are also severely lacking in provisions, medicine, and footwear. The dead are gone, and the wounded have no medicine for treatment. Eighty to ninety percent of the soldiers are in single layers of clothing and barefoot. We are fighting alone with no assistance. I hope you can contact various parties to provide our army with material assistance. I will now describe the recent battle situation again. At dawn yesterday, two enemy tanks, over ten armored vehicles, three hundred cavalry, and over a thousand infantry attacked the defense line of Xie's regiment at Liangdi Xing. After three hours of fierce fighting, they were bravely repulsed by our forces. Due to the deep snow of half a foot on the cold night, the enemy's armored vehicles were ineffective. We captured two armored vehicles and two mountain cannons, killing over a hundred enemies. According to captured enemies, each armored vehicle carries a mountain cannon, eight gunners, four light machine guns, and fifty shells. The Japanese bandits all use light machine guns, while the Mongols and defecting soldiers use rifles. They use cavalry to push the tanks and launch a fierce attack on all levels of command, with infantry continuing the attack. In this battle, our army lost two company commanders, four platoon leaders, three wounded platoon leaders, over fifty soldiers killed, and over seventy wounded. At dawn yesterday, about seven to eight hundred enemy cavalry attacked our left flank at Digoumen from Zhang Sanying. Our vehicles calmly fired, and after two hours of fierce fighting, the enemy retreated. We estimate that we killed over seventy enemy horses and captured three or four. Our army lost one platoon leader, eight soldiers killed, and thirteen soldiers wounded. In this battle, over a hundred enemies were killed. There have been no battles on the front lines today. According to intelligence, the enemy is gathering about ten thousand infantry, cavalry, and artillery, and over thirty tanks in the Zhang Sanying Tang Sanying area. I expect there will be a fierce battle tomorrow and the day after. In addition to ordering all units on the front lines to be on high alert, I am sending you this telegram. Sun Kuiyuan sealed.'"

Zhu Jiqing's Two Telegrams: Pan Yunchao, Director of the Shanghai Communications Office of the Northeast National Salvation Army Command Headquarters, received two telegrams from the headquarters yesterday as follows: (1) "Chen Lianfu, regimental commander of the [number] regiment of the [number] division of the Northeast National Salvation Army, upon receiving an order from Zhu Jiqing, led his division from a certain place to rush to the [blank] defense between Lengkou and Xifengkou to cooperate with a certain unit of the National Army in combat. Li Dianlin's unit of the [number] regiment is also under orders to prepare for mobilization." (2) "Telegram from the front lines on March 17: (1) The enemy stopped construction of the light railway from Jinchaolu Koubeiyingzi to Chaoyang County six days ago. (2) The enemy is transporting supplies from Chaoyang towards Chifeng, closer to Jianping and further back from Dahushan by ninety li compared to before. (3) The Daling River is currently thawing, making movement to the east and west inconvenient. We need to wait another two weeks for it to be passable."

Inner Mongolian Representative's Talk 131

Advocates for Reorganization of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission

Came to Shanghai the Previous Day to Meet Wang and Petition

Bai Rui, a resident of the Inner Mongolian leagues and banners in Beijing and currently serving as a supervisory committee member, De Kejih, a consultant to the Military Affairs Commission, and Liu Zhanyi of the Mongolian Culture Promotion Association came to Shanghai to welcome Wang Jingwei back to the country and to petition on Mongolian affairs. Yesterday morning, a reporter from the New Sound News Agency interviewed them at their hotel, asking about the current situation in Mongolia and their mission in Shanghai. They replied in detail as follows:

Inner Mongolian Leagues and Banners 132

Mongolia is divided into Inner and Outer Mongolia. Outer Mongolia has long been independent and is temporarily unrelated to the Central Government, so we will not discuss it for now. Inner Mongolia originally had six leagues, two independent banners, and two special departments. Each league has a different number of banners under its jurisdiction. The six leagues have a total of fifty-three banners. Including the independent banners and special departments, there are a total of fifty-seven banners, located in the western parts of Suiyuan, Chahar, Rehe, and the three northeastern provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang. The total population is approximately five million.

Half Already Lost 133

Since the September 18th Incident, the Northeast has fallen, and the Jerim League and Hulunbuir Special Department of the three northeastern provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, as well as the Ikmingan Independent Banner, have come under Japanese influence. With the fall of Rehe this year, the Juu Uda and Shilingol Leagues are also under enemy cavalry. Only the Xilingol, Ulaanchab, and Ih Juu Leagues and the Chahar Special Department, as well as the Tümed Independent Banner, remain within the borders of Chahar and Suiyuan provinces.

Mongolian Attitude 134

Although the leagues and banners in the three northeastern provinces have fallen to the enemy cavalry and are unable to resist due to the disparity in power, the Mongols' attitude towards Japan is extremely firm. The Japanese originally intended to organize a Manchurian-Mongolian puppet state, but because no Mongols were willing to be used, they were unable to realize it and only established the "Manchukuo." Later, representatives of the princes and nobles of the leagues and banners, aware of the crisis of the Japanese invasion of Rehe and Hebei, jointly went to Beijing in December of last year to petition for a plan to reorganize Inner Mongolia. The Central Government was also very concerned and expressed its sympathy.

Discord Between Top and Bottom 135

The highest organ in the Central Government in charge of Mongolian affairs is the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, but those who preside over the commission are unaware of the situation in Mongolia and seem indifferent to the rise and fall of Inner Mongolia. The suggestions of the representatives of the princes and nobles of the leagues and banners were shelved without any progress. Before and after the fall of Rehe this year, the leagues and banners also sent telegrams reporting and making suggestions, but they were all kept in the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission. Therefore, although the leagues and banners are grateful to the Central Government, they are disappointed that Mongolian affairs have not improved.

Petitioning Wang 136

We have come to Shanghai this time to welcome Mr. Wang Jingwei and to petition the Central Government to improve Mongolian policy, reorganize the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission, and eliminate the current state of [missing character] and to ensure that local opinions can reach the Central Government in order to bridge the gap. We met with Wang yesterday, and Wang expressed his strong approval.

League and Banner Organization 137

Although half of the leagues and banners in Inner Mongolia have fallen, the rest are also bordering war zones and are very dangerous. However, their attitude towards Japan is extremely firm, and they are unwilling to be subjugated. The league and banner system is a military organization. The basic unit is the Zuǒ, and the Zuǒlǐng commands five hundred able-bodied men. Four Zuǒ make up a Jia, with a Canlǐng. Each banner includes a different number of Jia, ranging from six or seven to over ten. The league is the annual meeting [missing character] of the banners, purely for military purposes. They also have considerable modern weapons and can be used.

Outer Mongolian Progress 138

Inner and Outer Mongolia are originally the same ethnic group, and their religions and customs are completely the same. Outer Mongolia has been independent for many years, and the government has always wanted to appease them, but this can only be effective after Inner Mongolia has a solution. Liu Zhanyi went to Outer Mongolia twice in 1924 and 1928 for investigation, and its politics, economy, and culture are thriving, showing the atmosphere of a new country. In contrast, Inner Mongolia is gradually declining. It is difficult to advocate for Outer Mongolia to return, and we sincerely hope that the Central Government will actively improve Inner Mongolia's administration as a foundation for recovering Outer Mongolia.

Wang Delin and His Family to Come to Shanghai 139

A Total of 166 People

Zhang Chuyu, the Shanghai representative of Wang Delin, the Commander-in-Chief of the Righteous Army of Heilongjiang Province, told a Far Eastern News Agency reporter yesterday that Wang Delin's family members departed from Dalian by ship on the 17th and will arrive in Shanghai within days. He also received a telegram from Commander Wang through Liang Yuanshan, the representative stationed in Beiping, requesting all agencies to assist in taking care of them. The original telegram is recorded as follows:

Recently, on the 16th of this month, I received a telegram from Commander-in-Chief Wang Delin stating: "Since the Japanese pirates have acted recklessly and established a puppet state, they have plundered the beautiful name of national self-determination and confused the world's audience. Are the descendants of the Chinese people willing to accept such humiliation? The people are aroused by righteous indignation and vow to resist to the death. Delin, awaiting punishment at the end of the military ranks, dares not lag behind. After years of bloody battles, we have killed more than ten thousand enemies, shattering the Japanese's deceptive lies. International public opinion has seen through their treachery. Since the national consciousness is known to all, Delin and others, though living in displacement and hardship, do not consider it bitter but rather sweet. Previously, due to the exhaustion of ammunition, I could not bear to let the women and children of the army perish with us, so I instructed them to temporarily enter Russian territory to await resettlement. Fortunately, the central government provided relief and sent ships to Vladivostok to welcome them back to the country. Surviving the tiger's mouth and seeing the glory of the Central Plains again is indeed a great fortune amidst misfortune. Recalling the compatriots trapped by the enemy, forced by violence, their laughter and tears are not their own, I feel even more urgently the responsibility of rescue. This time, returning to the country, there are a total of 188 wounded soldiers, women, and children. I have specially dispatched Zhao Shenyuan and Qu Tingfu to escort them on the ship southward. I have also telegraphed Representative Liang Yuanshan to make arrangements for their care in advance. The ship will transfer from Tianjin to Shanghai and is expected to arrive soon. I fear that they are unfamiliar with the place and that some unscrupulous individuals may take the opportunity to cause trouble. Therefore, the headquarters has issued certificates of identification, which they will hold separately, so that local officials can verify them at any time to avoid confusion. After landing, I earnestly request all charitable organizations and national salvation institutions to consider our displacement for the sake of the country and make proper arrangements for resettlement. If each of them can find their place, then the guarding officers and soldiers will be free from family burdens and will be more determined to kill the enemy and die for the country. This is specially communicated, respectfully requesting your kind attention." Upon receiving this telegram, it was found that there are 144 women and children, 25 men, and 19 wounded soldiers among the families of our army's generals, totaling 188 people. Except for the 19 wounded soldiers who will go to Beiping for medical treatment and the 11 family members of Brigade Commander Zhenxing who will come to Beiping, the remaining 166 family members will go directly to Shanghai. Accordingly, a telegram is sent to Shanghai agencies, requesting them to make extraordinary efforts to take care of them and ensure that they do not suffer from cold and hunger. This is our earnest hope."

He Xiangning and Others Initiate 141

Wartime Women's Service Training Class

Mayor Wu Requests Support Association to Allocate Funds to Help It Succeed

The Northeast Volunteer Army Support Association received a letter from Mayor Wu Tiecheng yesterday, along with the initiation charter of the Wartime Women's Service Training Class organized by the Women's Association, requesting financial assistance. Excerpts are as follows:

Wu's Letter 142

Mayor Wu Tiecheng's letter to the Support Association states: "I am writing to inform you that the war in the Northeast is becoming increasingly tense. It is difficult to predict how long the military situation will last or to what extent it will extend. The people of the country, united in mind and cooperating to fight the enemy, should make practical preparations to save themselves in order to achieve victory. The Chinese Women's Relief Association for Northeastern Compatriots is a powerful women's organization in our city. It has provided a great deal of donations and military supplies to the front lines. Now, the association plans to establish a Wartime Women's Service Training Class to train talents for long-term struggle, which is extremely important. However, the total cost of the military expenditure is six thousand yuan. Besides the association's responsibility to raise half of the amount, there is still a shortage of three thousand yuan. I have always admired your association's enthusiasm for saving the country and not lagging behind. Therefore, I have copied the initiation and charter of the association's Wartime Women's Service Training Class. I would like to request your association to allocate one thousand yuan to help its establishment. I hope that you will grant this request, and I will be extremely grateful."

Initiation 143

The initiation of the Wartime Women's Service Training Class, established by the Chinese Women's Relief Association for Northeastern Compatriots, states: "Since the fall of Yuguan and the danger to Beiping and Tianjin, the ambition of the brutal Japanese to annex China has become increasingly obvious. The future world situation is becoming more and more dangerous. The continuation of the current Sino-Japanese dispute is a harbinger of international war in the future. At that time, wars will be frequent and casualties are expected to be heavy. In the past European wars, the service of women in the rear was already remarkable. Today, the Japanese warlords have not only armed the youth of the whole country but also trained women. At this critical juncture of life and death in our country, if we do not quickly catch up and intensify preparations, we may not be able to find the time and opportunity to train women to participate in wartime services in the future. The original purpose of our association was to raise funds to help Northeastern refugees. However, as the recovery of the Northeast is uncertain and the Japanese continue to invade, it seems insufficient to only engage in passive relief. It is better to plan for active preparations for resisting the invasion, so as to take both into consideration and increase the effectiveness and sustainability. Therefore, we have specially passed the suggestion of Mr. He Xiangning to establish this training class, in order to train a part of enthusiastic and patriotic young women for the needs of long-term anti-Japanese resistance in the future. We hope that leaders from all walks of life and compatriots throughout the country will give material and spiritual support. This is our great hope."

Charter 144

(1) Purpose: In view of foreign aggression and the urgency of national crisis, the association has specially established a women's wartime rear service training class to train young women to undertake all kinds of services in the war zone and rear areas to facilitate the progress of the front-line war. (2) Organization: The class will establish a school affairs committee, with seven to nine members, elected by the executive committee of the Chinese Women's Relief Association for Northeastern Compatriots to handle all administrative matters. Under the school affairs committee, there will be two departments, teaching and administration, each with a director, a deputy director, a general secretary, and several staff members, responsible for handling daily teaching and administrative affairs. (3) Composition: The class will temporarily be divided into the following four groups according to the needs of the service scope: A. Rescue Group, B. Firefighting Group, C. Transportation Group, D. Sewing Group. (4) Enrollment: Each group will temporarily enroll 50 to 60 students, depending on the number of applicants selected. Two or three groups will be started first. (5) Curriculum: The required courses are temporarily set as follows (subjects may be added or supplemented as necessary): A. Rescue Group Required Courses: (1) Bandaging, (2) Pharmacology, (3) Disinfection, (4) First Aid Knowledge, (5) Nursing, (6) Poison Gas Protection Method, (Supplementary Courses) (1) Human Anatomy and Physiology, (2) Bacteriology, (3) Practice, (or others). B. Firefighting Group Required Courses: (1) Fire Prevention Method, (2) Firefighting Method, (3) Poison Gas Prevention Method, (4) Air Defense, (Supplementary Courses) (1) Introduction to Firefighting. C. Transportation Group Required Courses: (1) Wartime Knowledge, (2) Vehicle Driving Method, (3) Radio Transmission and Reception Method, (4) Air Defense Method, (5) Poison Gas Prevention Method, (6) Temporary War Zone Geography, (Supplementary Courses) (1) Military Training, (2) Mechanical Repair, (3) Others. D. Sewing Group Required Courses: (1) Hand Sewing, (2) Machine Sewing, (3) Military Uniform Tailoring Method (Military Supplies), (4) Medical Material Manufacturing Method, (5) Poison Gas Prevention Method, (Supplementary Courses) (1) Wartime Common Sense, (2) Others. In addition, experts will be invited to give one or two special lectures every week, focusing on domestic conditions, international situation, and other military, political, and economic common sense. (6) Duration of Study: The study period is temporarily set at six months for each group, and may be shortened as appropriate in case of urgent needs. Graduates with excellent grades in the final examination will be awarded a graduation certificate. (7) Study Period: The study period is temporarily set at three hours per day for each group (including practical time). It may be increased as appropriate, excluding the time for special lectures. (8) Teaching Materials: Teaching materials and handouts will be provided by the school. If there are no handouts, the teachers will dictate and the students will take notes. When using books, the students will pay for the books themselves. (9) Admission Procedures: All women of the Republic of China aged 16 or above, in good health, and with basic literacy, who fill out an application form, pass the examination and inspection, may be admitted as students of this school. (10) Discipline: All students are obliged to abide by the regulations of this school and the provisions of the application form, and shall not withdraw from school without a valid reason. They shall not evade service after graduation. (11) Funding: The necessary expenses shall be raised by the executive committee of the Women's Association. Tuition fees are waived. (12) Supplementary Provisions: If there are any matters not covered in this charter, the school affairs committee may revise them at any time.

Ministry of Communications Orders Post Offices 147

To Establish Temporary Post Offices in the Rehe Border Region

To Advance and Retreat with the Anti-Japanese Troops

According to news from the local post office, since the fall of Chengde, the post offices in Rehe Province have either been occupied by the Japanese army or have stopped operating. Now, in order to ensure the rapid transmission of news about the war, the authorities of the Ministry of Communications have specially ordered the post offices to establish temporary post offices within the anti-Japanese troops in the Rehe border region, to advance and retreat with the army, and to establish close contact. The procedures will be followed in accordance with the precedent of the postal blockade in the Northeast. After receiving the order, the post office has instructed the postal staff remaining in Rehe to quickly organize and establish them to facilitate military operations.

The customs will close the office and stop working on that day. All merchants are requested to comply. This is a special notice."

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Submits to Ministry of Finance 149

Request to Amend Import Tax on Newspapers

Change from Specific Duty to Ad Valorem Duty

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce submitted to the Ministry of Finance yesterday: "Submission Regarding a Request. It was found that on the 18th of this month, we received a letter from the Paper Industry Association stating that according to the import newspaper tax rate No. 513 of Category 10 promulgated by the National Government on December 29, 1930, (A) rolled paper is taxed at 1.5 yuan in customs gold per picul, and (B) other (i.e., packed) paper is taxed at 1.6 yuan in customs gold per picul. Later, in November 1932, the rolled newspaper was changed to 7.5% ad valorem, which was promulgated. It is found that the current price of each ton of newspaper in the market is about 86 yuan in customs gold. Calculated at 7.5% ad valorem according to item (A) of No. 513, the tax should be 6.45 yuan in customs gold. According to item (B), which is 1.6 yuan in customs gold per picul, each ton should be taxed at 26.88 yuan in customs gold, which is four times the difference. It is found that rolled paper is mostly used by large newspaper offices such as Shenbao and Xinwenbao, which have strong capital and complete equipment. Packed paper is mostly used by small newspaper offices in this and other cities with small capital for printing news and by bookstores for printing textbooks and books and magazines. The same goods, both necessities for cultural promotion, have different tax rates, which is not fair. Therefore, we hereby report this in writing and request your association to examine and approve this and forward it to the Tariff Commission of the National Government to amend the newspaper tax rate (A) and (B) of No. 513 in Category 10 to generally collect 7.5% ad valorem to avoid unevenness and eliminate abuses. It is a matter of public convenience. It was sent to the association. It is found that the import of newspapers is a cultural dissemination tool, and the tax should not be too high. In November of last year, it was stipulated that it should be 7.5% ad valorem, which is the purpose. However, the rolled newspaper has been changed to ad valorem tax, while the packed newspaper is still subject to specific duty. The same newspaper, but the packed newspaper is four times more taxed than the rolled newspaper, which is disadvantageous to the cultural industry with smaller capital. Therefore, it is necessary to correct it. It is reasonable to submit the matter in writing and request your department to examine and approve the change of the import tax of item B of No. 513 to ad valorem tax of 7.5% like item A, so as to eliminate prejudice and achieve public convenience."

Soviet Russian Industry Inspection Group 150

The Soviet Russian Industry Inspection Group is planned to be jointly organized by the government and the industry. Division of School Property Between City and County 151

The case of the division of educational property between Shanghai City and Shanghai County has been drafted and various solutions have been proposed. Therefore, the City Education Bureau sent a letter to the County Government requesting a date to jointly handle the handover procedures. After the County Government approved the letter, it immediately decided to transfer four-tenths of the ten mu and two fen and four li and five hao of the old school base to the city, which will be handled by the County Education Bureau. In addition, four-tenths of the base near Panfang will be transferred by the Property Management Office. The houses in the office were originally built by the Property Management Office. The county should receive 37%, which will be purchased by the city. The Property Management Office will estimate the price. The County Government has informed the City Education Bureau to schedule the handover procedures at 10:00 AM on March 20 (today) at the County Education Bureau on Shangwen Road.

Public Concession 152

Sanitary Conditions for the Previous Year

Liang Zhou Dengbo, the head of the Sanitation Department of the Public Works Department, reported on the 1932 fiscal year: "The public health conditions for this fiscal year, apart from the outbreak of cholera, were exceptionally good. The total number of deaths among foreign residents was only 567, which is 12.82 per thousand of the total population of 44,240. The previous year it was 17 per thousand, and the year before that it was 18.15 per thousand. The number of deaths among Chinese residents was 18,189, which is 17.65 per thousand of the total population of 1,032,0554. The previous year it was 16.71 per thousand, and the year before that it was 16.42 per thousand. The reason why this is higher may be that during the disturbances in this city, those who were seriously ill and returned to their hometowns at ordinary times could not go back at this time, so there were more deaths within the boundary. However, this report is still mostly incomplete, so its ratio is not accurate. As for cholera, although it was prevalent for a time, the total number of residents who died from this disease was only 162."

Infectious Diseases 153

The most important infectious disease this year was cholera, which reached its epidemic period at the end of April and disappeared after September 23. A total of 44 foreign patients were reported, and 13 died from it. 1544 Chinese patients were reported, and 149 died. Therefore, although the epidemic was severe, the number of deaths was not too large. After the epidemic started, chlorine gas disinfection was carried out in wells everywhere, and free clean water was supplied to residents in certain areas. At the same time, compulsory vaccination was carried out. According to the investigation, there is no real relationship between water wells and cholera, because most of the wells in the concession are not for drinking. Their existence may only be for feng shui reasons. Also, the spread of cholera does not coincide with the rise and fall of flies. In short, how this disease is transmitted is still difficult to say for sure. In addition to cholera, only smallpox and measles were slightly prevalent at the beginning of the year, and there is nothing much to pay attention to. In the past year, 200,210 people were vaccinated against cholera and 262,475 were vaccinated against smallpox.

Hospital Relocation 154

After the Sino-Japanese conflict broke out at the beginning of the year, the locations of the bureau-run hospitals were quite dangerous, and they were temporarily moved urgently. A total of five hospitals were moved to six locations. One of the largest was a warehouse, which was not prepared at all, but after three days, the layout was gradually completed. When moving, the procedures for moving patients and bedding were complicated, and the supervision could not be thorough. However, the patients were never affected, which shows the training and enthusiasm of the nursing staff. The loyalty of the low-level Chinese staff, who are not paid much, is especially commendable.

Refugee Problem 155

Since January, hotels and public facilities in the central district have become increasingly crowded with refugees. Smallpox and other diseases were spreading, and measures were taken to prevent them. However, supervision was not easy. Later, refugee shelters were established one after another, totaling 85, accommodating more than 44,000 refugees. There were also 26 wounded soldier hospitals, and the sanitation work was a heavy burden for the sanitation staff.

Veterinary Work 156

The work of the veterinary section is becoming increasingly heavy. Fortunately, at the beginning of this year, a Chinese veterinarian was added, so that systematic lung examinations could be carried out on dairy cows. Buffalo meat is now gradually under management, but goat meat has not yet been started due to religious reasons, and it needs to be carried out carefully. The method of eliminating diseased meat is now satisfactory.

As a result of the previous redistribution of personnel in small food shops, most of the small food shops are now also under management. Regarding the candies sold in these shops, some of which contained toxic pigments, after the crackdown, the larger shops have improved. However, the very small shops may not yet know the advantages and disadvantages. The results of this work are still satisfactory, but their effectiveness is not obvious.

School Inspections The sanitary conditions of some schools receiving subsidies from the bureau have been paid attention to. Because the number of sanitation staff has not increased, the initial inspections have not been completely satisfactory. Thanks to the Education Committee's power to grant and withhold, the situation has improved in most cases where the situation was particularly bad. However, this work is only a beginning today.

Import of Industrial Products from Various Countries Last Year 157

In the past year, my country purchased aircraft from various countries with a value of 1.33 million taels of customs gold, of which the United States accounted for 516,000 taels, France accounted for 208,429 taels, and the United Kingdom accounted for 604,372 taels of customs gold. The United States came with 1796 vehicles, the United Kingdom 746 vehicles, Germany 96 vehicles, Italy 49 vehicles, Japan 49 vehicles. United Kingdom made electrical equipment accounted for 7,322,154 taels, Japan 1,660,987 taels, and the United States 1,851,587 taels.

Dredging the Middle Section of the Puzhao River in Western Shanghai 158

Puhuitang Has Also Started Construction

The Caobing Outflow Changes from Longhua Port

Insufficient Dredging Funds Planned to Be Raised Again

Dredging the Puzhao River in Western Shanghai, the project is divided into three sections. The western section, which is already under construction, is under the jurisdiction of Songjiang and Qingpu counties, starting from Longzhu Temple in the west of Qibao Town and ending at Jiepai Bridge. The middle section starts from Jiepai Bridge to Tianyao Bridge, and has now been rerouted to Caobing Port and out of Longhua Port. The Municipal Works Bureau invited merchants to bid. The lowest bid price was 111,006 yuan, plus bridge and miscellaneous expenses, totaling more than 120,000 yuan. Because the funds, in addition to the 70,000 yuan allocated by the Post-War Committee of the Songhu War Zone, only had 30,000 yuan raised by Chen Yafu, a municipal commissioner in the Pusong area, and Cao Shen Yang Xinzheng, for a total of only 100,000 yuan. Therefore, the Municipal Works Bureau reduced the items one by one to more than 80,000 yuan, which, with the addition of bridge construction fees and office expenses, was just enough to reach 100,000 yuan. However, local people believe that the river has not been dredged for 24 years. If it is done sloppily and the bottom of the river is not dredged deeply, it will gradually silt up again after a few years. In order to seek a permanent solution, it is proposed to ask Chen Yafu and Yang Xinzheng to request the municipal authorities to raise funds for the shortfall and not approve the reduction. Now, on the one hand, dams are being built at both ends and dredging machines are being used to dredge. On the other hand, efforts are being made to raise funds again. The eastern section from Tianyao Bridge to Rihui Port has also been bid by the Municipal Works Bureau. The lowest bid price is 67,358.47 yuan. In addition to the 30,000 yuan allocated by the Post-War Committee of the Songhu War Zone, the French Public Works Bureau also subsidizes 15,000 taels of silver, which is about 21,000 yuan. The remaining shortfall will be raised by the Public Works Bureau, so construction can also begin soon.

New Shanghai County Government Construction Underway 159

The Sports Field is Taking Shape

Widening the Motor Road

Lawyer's Association General Meeting Postponed 160

April 16th

The Shanghai Lawyer's Association had originally scheduled its spring general membership meeting for 2:00 PM on the 26th of this month at the Lake Society, to elect all executive and supervisory committee members.
