Joint Announcement by Three Bureaus

The Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, Public Security Bureau, and Public Utilities Bureau jointly issued an announcement stating: "Regarding the matter of public announcement, this city has a large number of ships, merchants gather, and travelers come and go in droves. Every time a ship arrives at the port, tens of thousands of pieces of luggage are handled. Except for small, lightweight items that travelers can carry themselves, all heavier items rely on dock coolies for transportation. However, the number of coolies is large and complex, and there are often unscrupulous elements who collude with dock riffraff to defraud travelers, leading to forced carrying of luggage and extortion of fares. This has been heard of from time to time. If we do not find a way to rectify this, it will not be enough to reassure merchants and travelers. Therefore, this Bureau, etc., has jointly formulated the 'Registration Rules for Dock Coolies Handling Passenger Luggage' to handle the registration of coolies. It has been submitted to the Municipal Government and approved with Instruction No. 4799, stating that the submission and rules should be announced and implemented. Accordingly, we are copying and attaching the registration rules for public notice, so that all dock coolies handling passenger luggage at all docks will comply without fail. This announcement is attached with the 'Registration Rules for Dock Coolies Handling Passenger Luggage in Shanghai'. Article 1: All coolies who handle passenger luggage as a business at docks in this city must apply to the Public Security Bureau for registration. Article 2: Those within the area of the Shanghai South Shipping Dock must also comply with the regulations of the Public Utilities Bureau for managing docks in addition to these rules. Coolies applying for registration should first obtain five copies of the registration application form from the Public Security Bureau (one copy for the Social Affairs Bureau, two copies for the Public Security Bureau, and two copies for the Public Utilities Bureau), and submit them to the Public Utilities Bureau and Social Affairs Bureau for review. Dock coolies who handle passenger luggage who pass the review and receive an approval notice should personally bring a registration fee of one silver dollar and a stamp duty of one dime to the Public Security Bureau within seven days to obtain a registration certificate and uniform style. Article 4: Coolies should wear a uniform and carry a registration certificate when operating, so that they can be inspected by officials and police officers from the Public Security Bureau, Public Utilities Bureau, and Social Affairs Bureau at any time. They should also show the registration certificate to passengers before handling their luggage. Article 5: If passengers do not want to hire them, coolies must not forcibly carry their luggage or extort money by any means. Article 6: The rates for coolies handling passenger luggage are as follows, all calculated in silver dollars: small items 5 cents, medium items 10 cents, large items 15 cents. Article 7: Coolies must submit their registration certificate to the Public Security Bureau for cancellation when they cease operations, otherwise the guarantor will be held responsible for recovering it. Article 8: If a coolie loses their registration certificate, they must report it to the Public Security Bureau for reissuance and publish a statement in the newspaper declaring it invalid. Article 9: Registration certificates must not be lent or substituted. Violators will have their registration certificates revoked and be fined up to ten yuan. Article 10: Coolies' registration certificates should be submitted to the Public Security Bureau for renewal every July. Article 11: Violators of Articles , 5, and above will be sentenced to up to 15 days of detention or a fine of up to 15 yuan. In more serious cases, their registration certificates will be revoked. Article 12: Matters not covered in these rules may be submitted for amendment at any time. Article 13: These rules shall be implemented from the date of approval by the Municipal Government, March of the 22nd year of the Republic of China."

Public Security Bureau 165

Planning to Build a Memorial Monument and Cemetery 166

Wen Hong'en, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently noted that the number of officers and police officers under his command exceeds 5,000. Through diligent training, they have been able to fulfill their duties conscientiously. Over the years, many officers and police officers have been injured or killed by thieves, and during the January 28th Incident last year, those who died in battle alongside the military were particularly brave and sacrificed their lives. At a time of national crisis, they should be commended and recognized to serve as an example for future generations. Moreover, the remains of officers and police officers who have died from overwork and illness have lingered without being properly buried. He proposes to build a memorial monument to list the names of all officers and police officers who have died in the line of duty to honor their loyalty. At the same time, he also proposes to build a public cemetery to provide burial for officers and police officers who die in service and whose families cannot afford burial expenses, so as to console their souls. This will inspire those in service and provide peace to the deceased. Wen has submitted a report to Mayor Wu, explaining the reasons for building a memorial monument for officers and police officers who died in the line of duty and a police cemetery. He proposes to build the memorial monument in Longhua and the police cemetery in Pudong, requesting the Municipal Government to instruct the Land Bureau to allocate appropriate public land in the above two districts and to allocate construction funds of 100,000 yuan for construction.

Hui Chong Company Letter to the Support Association 171

Public Screening of Film to Donate to Volunteer Army

The Hui Chong Film Company sent a letter to the Support Association yesterday, offering to donate the total revenue from the first day of nationwide screenings of the film taken from the Northeast to the volunteer army. The original letter stated: "The country is in great difficulty, and all people should do their best to serve the country. Hui Chong deeply knows that film has the ability to promote propaganda. The facts of the enemy being killed in front are also what the people in the rear should know in detail. Therefore, last year, it came to Shanghai from Guan, uniting with Mr. Ren Xifan and Ren Jinpin to form a frontline photography team. Going north out of Guan to take pictures on the spot, the volunteer army that has been automatically dispersed by the bitter battle in front, makes them meet with our people in the rear on the screen, or even further make people in countries other than the enemy see the truth of the front line, fully showing the spirit of self-determination of our nation, and the evil propaganda that is now falsely accused of being bandits becomes a worthless rumor. There are even those who say that now is the struggle between countries, and the national soldiers and civilians must unite and fight together to resist the enemy. Then the enemy country with 70 million people will be restrained by the Korean revolutionary patriots, and under the efforts of the 477 million people in the whole country, the last collapse will be reaped. Hui Chong has traveled all over the front line, and feels that the volunteer army he has seen are all daredevils, and the bold words of Lao Beifeng and Zhang Haitian that there are no enemy soldiers in their eyes are especially inspiring. General Sun Dianying met Hui Chong in Chengde, which has now been lost, when Hui Chong had finished filming the volunteer armies of Feng Zhanhai, Tang Juwu, and Wang Huayi and returned. His determination to resist the enemy to the death can be seen in the spirit of his troops enduring hardship. The Sun army's clothes are all thin, and the daily food is only worth a few cents, but because they are eager to save the country, they all do not think it is bitter, and each encourages the other to kill an enemy if they die, and capture an enemy if they live. On the way of the Sun army to Chifeng Weichang, General Sun smiled and told Hui Chong, 'In the near future, please take pictures of me capturing a thousand prisoners from the enemy.' And in the Battle of Chifeng on March 1, he personally witnessed the enthusiasm of his troops in battle and their bravery in killing the enemy. No one who sees it will not respectfully cry and admire it. Now, our team is planning to go out of Guan for the second time. Before going out of Guan, we will first screen the films we have taken to promote propaganda, and we are willing to donate all the income from the first day of screenings in all theaters across the country to your association and the Northeast Hardship Relief Association. The donated funds will be used to purchase necessary items, with one-half to assist General Sun and one-half to assist the volunteer armies of various departments. Please assign personnel from your association to discuss the method of collecting the funds. Colleagues share the people's concerns. This is to strive to promote propaganda work and to make a sign of assistance to the frontline soldiers, and we hope that all sectors of the country will unite to assist the volunteer army and the frontline soldiers who are fighting hard, and with the spirit of military-civilian cooperation, assist the government to resist foreign enemies, so that the enemy's military power will be reduced day by day, and the lost land of our country will be returned in time. The letter does not convey all the meaning. It is heard that the Support Association has appointed Chen Yafu to be responsible for the handling."

County Government 172

Deadline for Taibao Female Shamans to Change Occupation

The Shanghai County Government has found that within the county, Taibao female shamans are generally borrowing from ghosts and gods to deceive the people. Such superstitious practices are detrimental and should be strictly prohibited. In addition to issuing notices to all public security bureaus to investigate and prohibit such activities, a notice has also been issued stating that all those engaged in Taibao female shamanism must change their occupations within two months. After the deadline, if they are discovered again, both those who invite the Taibao female shamans and those who practice Taibao female shamanism will be summoned and punished without leniency.

Zhengtai Factory Submits Report on Continued Payment of Compensation 176

The Zhengtai Rubber Factory No. 1 on Tangshan Road in this city, unfortunately, suffered a fire due to an electrical fault last month. Details have been reported in this newspaper. It is now known that the factory has provided generous compensation to the families of the deceased and the injured workers. Because the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau needed to know the details of the aftermath, it ordered the factory to continue to report. The factory has now submitted a written report on the aftermath yesterday. The original text is as follows: "Submitting a report on the handling of the aftermath of the disaster at our factory, requesting your approval for record-keeping. Previously, our factory suffered a tragedy in which an electrical short circuit caused a steam boiler to explode, killing 82 male and female workers. In the aftermath of the disaster, our factory worked hard to handle the funeral arrangements and compensation for the families of the deceased, etc. The details have been reported to your office for review and approval. This sudden disaster was an act of God, and human power could not have prevented it. Our factory suffered huge losses and was almost on the verge of collapse. However, considering that the workers died in the line of duty, it is pitiful. In addition to giving each family a compensation fee of 300 yuan, we have now tried our best to raise funds to give each family an additional 50 yuan, in the hope of comforting the spirits, and the families of the deceased can also understand the difficult situation of our factory. There are no objections, and all have signed and received the full amount. It is reasonable to submit a supplementary report, requesting your review and approval for record-keeping. This would be a great kindness. Respectfully submitted to Wu, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Social Affairs Bureau."

County Agricultural Education Hall Advocates Forming a 177

Association to Abolish Tomb Sweeping Day Burning

Members Must Follow Discipline

Declare Names and Pay Fines

The Shanghai County Farmers' Education Hall, in order to promote the abolition of the bad habit of burning during Tomb Sweeping Day, specifically raised the issue for discussion at the 178th Hall Affairs Meeting. It was decided to organize an association to promote the abolition of Tomb Sweeping Day burning. Those who wish to join must fill out an application form and find a guarantor. The regulations of the association are recorded below: (1) This association is organized to promote thrift and eliminate superstition, and is named the Association to Abolish Wasteful Tomb Sweeping Day Burning. (2) Those who meet the following qualifications and wish to join this association must fill out an application form and find a guarantor: (A) Those who reside within three miles of Zhuanqiao. (B) Those who are 14 years of age or older. (3) Members of this association and their families must absolutely abolish burning during Tomb Sweeping Day, except for direct ancestors. (4) Members of this association are responsible for urging and monitoring. (5) Once a member joins this association, they cannot withdraw. (6) Members of this association shall mutually elect three directors to handle daily affairs. (7) For the convenience of handling affairs, this association is divided into two sections: documentation and enforcement, and finance. Each section is headed by a director, concurrently held by a director. (8) If a member of this association or their family members cannot abide by the regulations of this association and secretly burn paper money, the association will deal with them in accordance with the following provisions: (A) If a member or their family member secretly burns paper money and is witnessed by a member of the same association, in addition to the incineration of the paper money, a fine of four dimes will be imposed. (B) If a family member of a member secretly burns paper money and is reported by someone and there is evidence, in addition to the incineration of the paper money, a fine of three dimes will be imposed. (C) If a member or their family member secretly burns paper money and is a repeat offender, the penalty will be doubled. (D) If a member or their family member violates the rules of this association five times, their name will be announced. (9) If a member does not comply with the penalty rules of this association, the guarantor will be responsible. (10) The fines paid by members will be kept by the finance section, and when they reach a certain amount, they will be used to fund the Zhuanqiao rest clock. (11) The expenses of this association will be borne by the founders. (12) This association is affiliated with the Zhuanqiao Farmers' Education Hall in Shanghai County. (13) These regulations shall be implemented after being passed by the Hall Affairs Meeting and submitted to the county for record-keeping.

Trial of Criminals Who Kidnapped a Young Child 179

Jiang Desheng, a local resident who lives at No. 45 Jianye Li, Fulvli Road, in the French Concession and works at the Western District Office of the Shanghai Telephone Company on Bixun Road, had his six-year-old son, Jiang Atang, kidnapped while playing in the alley on February 13th at 3:00 PM. The kidnappers sent a letter to the victim, demanding a ransom of 15,000 yuan for his release. The victim sent his neighbor, Chen Abing, to negotiate with the kidnappers. Because the kidnappers demanded an exorbitant amount, the matter was not resolved. It was not until the evening of the 16th of this month that Jin Jiulin, a special detective of the French Concession Police, learned that the two parties were negotiating in Room 22 of the Huayang Hotel on Guangxi Road. He immediately led detectives to arrest the kidnappers, Zhou Liansheng and Zhang Hualang. Later, they successively arrested accomplices Fei Zhaoshi and Wang De and searched a pavilion room at No. 30 Wulili on Tokyo Road, finding the female bandit, Shouzhen, and Zhang Jiangxiang, bringing the total number of arrested male and female bandits to six, and taking them to the police station for questioning. The police transferred the criminals to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District yesterday, where Judge Li Changnian conducted the trial. The police lawyer, Yao Zhaodi, stated that the defendants were arrested for kidnapping and extortion, but the main criminal was still at large and the case was complex, so the police had not yet completed a detailed investigation. He requested a postponement of three weeks to allow for a thorough investigation before filing the prosecution. After the court briefly questioned the defendants, it approved the postponement until the next trial on April 7th. The defendants were remanded to custody.

Wang Jiliang Commits Suicide Due to Poverty 181

Life of Thrift Leads to Suicide

Leaves Ten Letters Entrusting Wife to Friends and Relatives

Wang Jiliang, a Shanghai native, was 34 years old. His wife, Zhang, was 29 years old and from Ningbo. They had two sons and one daughter: the eldest son, Benquan, was 7 years old, the second daughter, Meimei, was 5 years old, and the youngest son, Benin, was just 1 year old. The family lived together at No. 7, Liujialong, Sanpailou, in the city. Wang used to work as a clerk in the British-owned Gongyu Fire Insurance Company but was later dismissed due to some incident. Although he tried to find a job through referrals, he was unsuccessful, and he has been unemployed at home for many years. Usually, there was no income, and the family was large, with huge monthly expenses, so life became increasingly poor. Overwhelmed by depression, he suddenly had the idea of committing suicide. Yesterday morning at around 5:00 AM, Wang got up. Zhang knew that Wang was usually very thrifty at home, and he would get up every day at dawn to wipe the windows and sweep the floor, so she did not suspect him even though he got up a little early yesterday morning, and she remained in bed. At around 8:00 AM, she suddenly heard a loud knocking on the door. She was startled and called Wang to go and open the door. However, she called him repeatedly but received no response. She quickly got out of bed to investigate, but she saw that Wang had hanged himself on the beam and had been dead for a long time. There was no way to bring him back to life. She was greatly shocked and ran out immediately to open the door, where she saw that the visitor was a relative from the countryside. She invited the relative inside, but the relative was also stunned upon seeing the situation. Zhang cried loudly over the body. The incident was then reported to the Second Office of the First District, and Director Liu dispatched Police Chief Li Fuyi to investigate. Because it involved a death, he ordered the local head to report it to the Shanghai Local Court for an autopsy. It is said that Wang wrote ten letters before his death, instructing his wife to distribute them to his relatives and friends. The main content of the letters was to entrust them to take care of his widow and young children.

Moving a Ladder Leads to Death 182

Pitiful Demise of Fan Xingyou

Fan Xingyou, a Ningbo native and owner of a tobacco and paper shop named "Tong Kang," located at the Jian De Li intersection on Ou Jia Road in Hongkou, was fifty years old. Yesterday, around 12 PM, he went to the second floor of his shop to hold a child. His wife, forgetting he was upstairs, moved the small, portable ladder. Shortly after, Fan casually walked downstairs, lost his footing, and fell, severely injuring his head. He lost consciousness. His family rushed him to Tongren Hospital, but attempts to save him were unsuccessful, and he died around 3 PM.

Reader's Advisor 190

On the Question of "What is China's Illness?"

Reply to Mr. Pu Bingjun of Jiangyin and Mr. Bo Chaoyu of Nanjing: We have received letters from Mr. Pu Bingjun of Jiangyin and Mr. Bo Chaoyu of Nanjing in response to our discussion of the question "What is China's illness?" sparked by Mr. Shen Zuguang's letter. The two gentlemen criticized us for only pointing out the inaccuracies in Mr. Shen's words and not providing him with a sincere answer "from the advisor's standpoint." Mr. Bo even more vehemently described our debate as "irrelevant, pointless, and completely unrelated to the topic, a truly laughable and alarming argument." While we do not blame Mr. Bo for his vehement and even slightly fearful tone, we believe that if there were more readers like Mr. Bo, our reader's advisor would have already had a significant impact on the public and garnered widespread attention. Even if this reporter were truly "alarming," he would die content in his grave. However, no matter how loudly Mr. Bo shouts "alarming" and "laughable," we must still fulfill our advisor's duty. As the saying goes, "While there is still breath, this ambition must not be slackened." Although our attitude in replying to Mr. Shen was sometimes too severe, it cannot be said to be insincere. On the contrary, it was precisely because we were so sincere that we unknowingly expressed a strict attitude. The question "What is China's illness?" was the title given by the editor of this column in response to Mr. Shen's letter and our reply. In fact, this title is the fundamental question discussed in Mr. Shen's letter and is not, as Mr. Bo claims, "completely unrelated to the topic." This is point one. Our reply to Mr. Shen's letter focuses solely on pointing out his errors, not because we are inherently "argumentative" or "fond of literary flourishes," but because it is our style as a reader's advisor to answer questions in a way that is engaging, enlightening, and educational. I recall a famous European philosopher, a relatively young university professor (which is almost an exception in Europe). Although he was a scholar of Neo-Kantian idealism and a reformist, he had fiercely opposed war in Europe. He had many followers and a kind of organization. Once, at their annual meeting, after the university professor gave a report, he asked each member present to raise questions. He would never answer the questions immediately but would instead relentlessly and mercilessly pursue the questioner's own opinions on the question they had raised. Only when the questioner's opinions on the issue had been "exhausted" and there was no room for evasion would he then slowly express his own opinion, leaving the audience enlightened, as if they had drunk sweet nectar. Sometimes, members were pursued to the point of being speechless and even crying, but he would never stop questioning or change his relentless attitude because of these situations. This is similar to studying mathematics. If a difficult math problem arises and one immediately asks the teacher, who immediately tells him the method of calculation, then he will not deeply understand the explanation of the formula for this difficulty. Only after he has put in some thought, tried various methods, and found them all to be "dead ends" will he then gain a thorough understanding after the teacher points out the solution. Moreover, his previous hard work is a necessary process for his current thorough understanding; without the previous hard work, there will be no subsequent thorough understanding. This reporter is not talented, but I have secretly adopted this approach in dealing with readers ("Am I fond of arguing? I have no choice.") This is point two. Mr. Shen's views on national politics in his letter are completely influenced by the prevailing corrupt theories and are deeply prejudiced. That is to say, unless he is relentlessly pursued to the point of "having nowhere to hide" and "having nothing to say" and admits his own mistakes, he will not understand or accept our positive explanation of the problem. This is point three. Moreover, in the process of debate, we can see each other's fundamental views on this issue without waiting for the respondent to formally reply. Having said this, we still need to discuss the opinions of the readers before publishing our own opinions. Perhaps at that time, we only need to make a conclusion to what we have debated. Now, let us first study Mr. Bo's diagnosis of "What is China's illness?" Mr. Bo said, "As for what China's illness is, I can give a simplest and most clear answer, which is in a single thought of the four hundred million people." This is to say that China's illness lies in the fact that the four hundred million people do not have a single thought. Then, we must ask Mr. Bo: Why do the four hundred million people of China not have this "single thought?" Who is preventing them from having this single thought? Is it God? Then we should advise the public to go to church to pray. This cannot solve the problem. They are all doing somersaults in the clouds of idealism and are indeed the same. How can China be saved without changing their minds? Why can't the four hundred million people all work together to "have a single thought?" Is there any "calling the wind and summoning the rain" or "scattering beans to form soldiers" kind of mystery here? If not, please tell us where it is. If not, then we still need to pursue the "social causes" and its material causes, namely the economic causes, that prevent our four hundred million people from being able to "change their minds." If this kind of fantasy that goes up to the heavens and down to earth - the idea of "a single thought" - is not fundamentally eliminated, we will tell you that you will not believe where China's illness lies. Even if we take a step back and admit that there is some reason in what you say, it only speaks of China's symptoms but does not see the root of China's illness. This is point four. In fact, Mr. Bo has unconsciously stated the root of China's illness. Didn't Mr. Bo say: "What stage has China reached now? Foreign aggression is becoming more urgent, internal affairs are not being improved. Although the political authorities' opinions are temporarily cooperating because of the national crisis, can they ultimately cooperate until the end? In addition, natural disasters, man-made disasters, the penetration of imperialism, the bankruptcy of the rural economy, education, politics, especially finance, are full of holes!"? Aren't these "illnesses?" Can anyone deny that these are not China's illnesses? But since we want to cure the illness, we cannot treat the head when it hurts or the foot when it hurts. We must pursue where the root of the illness lies and then use the method of "hitting the snake at its seven inches" to make a fundamental attempt at treatment in order to be effective. Mr. Bo mentioned these symptoms, but who is the main illness, who is the secondary illness, who is the illness of the heart and abdomen, and who is the disease of the skin? Naturally, Mr. Bo did not have time to think deeply. However, from Mr. Bo's diagnosis of China's illnesses, we have already found a half-close diagnosis of the source of the illness, which is "the penetration of imperialism and the bankruptcy of the rural economy." The so-called imperialism is the political form of the final stage of the financial capital force of international capitalism. The bankruptcy of China's rural areas is the result of the intrusion of this imperialist force. If we want to understand the location of this root of the disease, we must: (1) study the relationship between international economic politics and China's economic politics; (2) study the historical achievements of the rulers of advanced capitalist countries and the modern fate and material causes of the actions of the rulers of colonies; (3) the history and prospects of the struggles of the international commoners or the poor masses. If everyone can patiently study these three things sufficiently, then their observation of China's problems and international problems will certainly be different from the current concept of "swallowing dates whole." At that time, when you come to observe China's phenomena, you will find that many things that you previously thought were strange are now a historical necessity, and you will find their answers. For example, the League of Nations cannot solve the Sino-Japanese dispute. Not only can it not solve the Sino-Japanese dispute, but we have long shouted loudly, but at that time everyone turned a deaf ear. What is it like now? Aren't all of our "fortunately getting it right" verified everywhere? In fact, as long as you are willing to calmly study the three methods we pointed out earlier, you will definitely come to this conclusion. This is point five. Mr. Bo's views are really too unclear, and there are many places to discuss. However, just from this, it has already become a long article, so we will stop here and talk about it later.

Jinan and French Business P] Jinan won 4-2 Outcome: 4-4 Draw Jinan's Outstanding Performance is a Pity 191

Yesterday, in the West League football match between Jinan and French Business at Yiyuan, Jinan won enthusiastic applause from the audience with its clear and wonderful performance. Although there were only a little over a thousand spectators, each and every one was very satisfied and triumphant, resulting in a 4-4 draw. However, Jinan's ball control always held the upper hand, and they once led 4-2. Because they conceded two penalty kicks in a row, the game ended in a draw. A pity for Jinan!

The game started with both sides exchanging attacks, each creating dangerous moments, but neither side managed to score. After about twenty minutes of play, Pan Haiguang received the ball seventeen or eighteen yards from the opponent's goal, raised his foot and swept a shot. The ball was sharp and fast, rolled along the ground, and penetrated the corner of the net. It was a beautiful sight. The goalkeeper dived to save it but failed. Jinan thus opened the scoring first. French Business

French Business's football skills are not to be trifled with. They once drew 4-4 with Agal. Although Jinan scored a goal, it did not dampen their spirit. The French player Fa Fanque broke through on the flank and passed the ball in front of the goal. In the ensuing melee, Jinan's Lai Zuorong was penalized for a handball, and French Business's center-back Remy Dy converted the penalty, making it 1-1. Jinan Two

After the tie, the center kick was taken again, and Jinan launched a vigorous attack, directly threatening the goal. They were as fierce as dragons and tigers, full of vigor. Luo Haiguang shot a high ball, which the goalkeeper Fu Lushu caught. Zhang Hongzao quickly followed up, and the goalkeeper, in a moment of carelessness, let the ball slip from his grasp and roll into the net. Jinan thus took the lead again, 2-1. French Business Two

Thereupon, Jinan's momentum grew stronger, and the forwards were extremely active. The situation in front of the French Business goal changed rapidly, and the atmosphere was tense. Once, Jinan's Jin Yongsen shot very quickly, but unfortunately, it went wide. French Business turned bad luck into good, launched a counter-attack, and their left inside forward, Walter, shot from a distance towards the goal. The ball was as fast as an arrow, and Xu Heng failed to save it, resulting in a 2-2 tie, ending the first half. Jinan Three

As the second half began, Jinan attacked from the right flank. Zhong Yongsen, like a four-horse chariot, dribbled the ball deep, reaching the edge of the goal before passing it in front. The left winger Wang Nanzhen rushed up quickly and shot fiercely at the goal, but was unfortunately blocked by the goalkeeper. As one wave subsided, another rose again. Zhong Yongsen delivered a wonderful corner kick, and Liang Shutang headed it towards the goal. The goalkeeper caught the ball, but Fu Hexuan saw an opportunity and rushed up. The goalkeeper couldn't dodge in time, and the ball slipped into the net again. Jinan Four

Not long after the match resumed, Jinan's Yun Fengyun was kicked in the temple by Ke Laituo and left the field to apply medicine. Jinan continued to work hard. Luo Hai was magnificent and unstoppable, launching a series of attacks and achieving another great feat. Jinan then led 4-2, thinking they could secure the victory. However, fortunes change unpredictably. From then on, Jinan was at a disadvantage everywhere, and bad luck struck. The situation changed completely. French Business Three

Despite this setback, French Business's morale did not wane. Instead, they showed more energy and greater vigor. Fa Fanque forced a corner kick, which was well delivered. In the ensuing melee in front of the goal, the situation was chaotic, and the ball somehow sneaked into the net amidst the crowd. The Jinan players looked at each other in silence, not knowing what had happened. As a result, French Business's momentum grew stronger, and they pressed hard. Xu Heng walked over the ball, and Jinan conceded another free kick, not far from the goal. Fortunately, it didn't go in. French Business Four

French Business continued to press, coming on strong. Jinan's formation suddenly looked flustered. Unfortunately, they conceded another penalty kick, which Remy Dy converted again, making it a 4-4 draw. Afterwards, Jinan launched another attack, and Zhang Hongzao was the first to arrive, shooting at the empty goal, thinking that the opponent's goal would fall in an instant. However, the ball rolled out of the goal. The audience was very disappointed. The final whistle blew, and on the way home, one could still hear fans expressing their regret. The referee was Zhang Le. The Bloody Account of Spring and Autumn Sun Wenlan

Two people had a fight in the house. Of course, there was considerable damage to both bodies and property; however, comparatively speaking, the owner always suffers! If, when the fight subsides, the outsider quietly runs away, there is nothing to be done about it. But if he turns around and demands compensation from the owner for bodily harm, that is truly the most ridiculous thing. According to Japanese news, there is now a man named Naito Juntaro in their country who has published a book entitled "Settlement of the Manchurian-Mongolian (Blood) Account." This is truly a far-fetched and absurd way to settle an old debt. Originally, the Japanese occupation of the three northeastern provinces was like a rogue entering someone's house. With the family (not resisting), he trashed the living room and claimed it as his own. However, he himself was careless and tripped over the threshold! Or he missed a step and broke his head (shedding blood). Not only does he not compensate for the losses, but he turns around and extorts money, wanting to settle this (blood) account. I think Naito Kotaro truly deserves to be a Japanese citizen; his thinking is indeed more comprehensive. That is why he has this book, "Settlement of the Manchurian-Mongolian Blood Account," to assist their government in ways they hadn't thought of. Fine! (It's good to have an account to settle), this is something that no one will lose out on. The lives and property of our northeastern people, as well as the nation's military supplies, airplanes, soldiers, etc., are all sacrificed at their hands! Since we are talking about settling accounts, even if we deduct the price we should pay him for (blood), we should still ask him to compensate us another 400 million taels of silver, and that might not be enough! Friends, remember! This immeasurable account of losses still deserves our efforts to settle with him!

Soccer Game Yongzi

Who Will Win the Championship?

Since the big soccer game between the German team and the Allied team from 1914 to 1918, until the first half of 1931, except for a few unremarkable friendly matches, we soccer fans who are not afraid of bloodshed have not seen a formal soccer match for a long time. How fortunate! In the second half of 1931, the Japanese team, eager to try their skills, challenged the Chinese team at the Northeastern Sports Field. Logically, this match should have been quite a spectacle, but unexpectedly, the Chinese team was truly inadequate. As soon as they took the field, they only defended and did not attack. The ball kept spinning around the Chinese team's goal, and the goalkeeper was unwilling to put in some effort. The ball repeatedly rolled into the goal through the gaps in his legs, creating a one-sided situation. Although the match has not yet finished, it seems that the Chinese team has no hope of winning the champagne. Good news has spread that the German team, which was defeated by the Allied team before, is not reconciled and has been very active these past few days. They are eager to regroup, issue a challenge to the Allied team, and have another decisive battle. Upon investigation, the German team's soccer skills were far superior to those of the Allied team in the previous match. After the kickoff, the German team had smooth sailing, with a tendency to directly attack the enemy's base. The Allied team saw that this was not the way to go, so they pulled in the American goalkeeper, and their military strength suddenly increased. They turned defense into offense and turned defeat into victory, snatching the champagne back from the German team's hands. The German team is a world-renowned soccer team, and the Allied team is the previous champion of the champagne. If these two teams intend to compete again at the European Sports Field, it goes without saying that it will be much more exciting than the match between the Japanese team and the Chinese team. Moreover, both sides have been recuperating for a long time and are bound to have a performance that is novel to an unknown degree, winning the audience's praise and causing them to be amazed. The competition at the Northeastern Sports Field has come to an end, while the one at the European Sports Field has not yet begun. Soccer fans, please be patient.

Shanghai City Ke Ding

Like a Kaleidoscope Full of Unpredictable Changes!

In the morning, I got out of bed at six-thirty and put on my clothes. Walking on the road, I couldn't see the bright lights and the bustling crowds of men and women from the previous night. I only saw the hazy fog in front of me and smelled the foul odor attacking me. Then there were the night soil collectors slowly pushing their carts, and the coolies dragging their carts forward. Other than that, there were only two or three police officers loitering on the street. If you haven't been to Wangping Street in the morning, then you should take a trip there. Because that place has become a unique "newspaper market" in Shanghai. From the front of the Shenbao newspaper office all the way to both ends of Wangping Street on Fourth Road, it is the world of newspaper vendors. Before six o'clock, they are all busy going to the newspaper office to get the newspapers. After they get them, some of them, probably the whole family, come out. Everyone folds the newspapers and sorts them in an orderly manner to wait for their customers. After seven o'clock, it is their busiest time for business. Some of the female owners count the copper coins and pack them up, piling them up in packages to exchange for silver dollars or banknotes. It is said that their daily profit is always above that of a middle-level employee! Friends who are inexperienced in the world, thinking of coming to Shanghai to play, or coming to Shanghai for some business, find it difficult to bring a lot of luggage. As soon as you get off the train, you feel the difficulty. The luggage has already been sent from the platform to outside the station. At this time, you really have some trouble. The shouting of hotel porters, the solicitation of rickshaw pullers, and the noise of chauffeurs and coachmen simply make your head spin. At the same time, there are some people who offer their services to carry your luggage. If you are not careful, your luggage may be pushed and squeezed by them and eventually disappear. There are also some people who see that you have a lot of luggage that you can't carry yourself, and they invite you to hire a car. You agree on the price with him, and he goes to call a rickshaw. Then he asks you for money, and also pays the rickshaw puller, but you only pay half. This is the rickshaw broker, he earns commissions. Trying to save money by buying a watch on the street from someone wearing an old military uniform is simply a big rip-off. Because, based on my experience, there is such a person on Nanjing Road who is always selling watches. However, he says: "I was injured in the military and have no other choice, so I have to sell this watch." According to insiders: (This is a scam!)

Saying and Doing Tu Hongxia

Chinese People Who Can Only Talk and Not Do

Yesterday, I ran to a friend's house and saw a study schedule he had made for himself, from four o'clock in the morning until twelve o'clock in the afternoon. Except for school and meal times, there was hardly any time left. This kind of hardworking and persevering spirit is indeed admirable. When I asked him about it, his younger sister interjected and said: "Except for school, he has never even opened a book. Do you think his schedule is good?" He heard this, his face turned red, and he remained silent. I think, in China, whether it is a big matter or a small matter, it is viewed in this way: because talking big is the genius of the Chinese people. They say things that are earth-shattering, but do nothing. If there is no proof, please look at the facts: three people form a partnership to open a tofu shop. When they organize it, they ask an intermediary to set many conditions, everyone should work hard and jointly seek the development of the business. But, in the end, A takes the money to gamble every day, B takes the money to visit prostitutes every day, and C, seeing their actions, also learns from them. As a result, there is no business at all, the ashes on the tofu press are an inch thick, and the tofu pot is covered in rust. When the head of an organization takes the stage, he does nothing else. As soon as his luggage is laid out, the first step is to announce future plans, saying things that are ten thousand miles away from reality, but as long as it sounds good, there is no need to worry about whether it can be done, because (saying) is a duty, and (doing) is a favor. Why? The theorem is like this: (not saying and doing) is a fool, (saying and doing) is an idiot, (not saying and not doing) is waste, only (saying and not doing) is the most brilliant. Because there are too many extremely brilliant people in China, everything in China is a mess. Alas! Smart people!

Four pots of red plum blossoms and two pots of green wheatgrass were placed around the tea table. Women's Paradise Women's Cry Hui Shu

I don't like to hear women say self-consoling words: "I am unlucky to be born a woman!" Women can also be independent, and can also govern their families and countries. Mothers Must Know Juan Yun

Taking care of children is the most tiresome and annoying thing. Young children are as delicate as gold watches, and must move forward in a prescribed manner. Eating is a crucial aspect for children. It should not be too active, nor should it be too lazy. There are many mothers who, because their child was sickened by oranges, will never let their child eat oranges again. This method seems too stupid. (Take care of children with three parts hunger and three parts cold.) This is an old saying, and it has a lot of truth to it. Children from wealthy families are always unwilling to be cold or hungry, and often get sick. Impoverished children who endure hunger and cold are just as lively and healthy, and have no problems at all. Children like to make noise for no reason, and naturally feel bored and lonely. Mothers should use novel and attractive methods to distract them. There are those who advocate giving them a beating, which is enough to increase the child's bad feelings and is not smart.

Regarding Maternity Yun

Giving birth to a child is a major difficulty for women, so-called (one foot in the coffin, one foot outside the coffin.) Especially for the first birth, this is what everyone thinks in their heads. During the ten months of pregnancy, different changes occur in each part, the uterus's elasticity stretches and shrinks, and the nerves suffer a lot of trauma. It seems that after a woman becomes pregnant, she should wear a tight-fitting belly band on her stomach. Wearing a belly band is not because she dislikes the big belly being inconvenient, but to help the child come down easily during future childbirth. The most taboo thing in midwifery is to allow stagnant blood to enter the uterus, causing dangerous metritis. In Western medicine, for inflammation in postpartum women, they advocate using ice packs, but the result of this experiment has already killed many poor postpartum women! Often, taking some Chinese medicine that is peaceful, although it delays the time a little, there are many who can be saved. Perhaps it is because the constitution of Chinese people is different from that of Westerners. No matter how strong the body has always been, it is absolutely not advisable to move around within two weeks after childbirth. If, three days after childbirth, the doctor proves that there is no illness, then you can slightly get up. Open the windows, take deep breaths; or lie flat on the bed, straighten your toes, and tighten your legs, raise your body once, and then slowly relax. This simple exercise helps the growth of muscle tissue and gradually restores the original state before pregnancy. In any case, postpartum women must have considerable protection and hygiene everywhere after pregnancy. Dangerous facts are mostly caused by negligence and lack of hygiene!

Chapter 4: The Situation of Business (Continued) Discussing the business of experts in each department, of course, surgery is the best, and internal medicine is the worst, because society still has a deeply ingrained impression that (Western medicine is good for surgery, and Chinese medicine is good for internal medicine.) Moreover, surgical operations are indeed effective and obvious. However, those who die after unsuccessful surgical operations are also very miserable. Surgeons who are not good at surgery cannot pretend to be good. Surgeons cannot perform their business without a good operating room. Before the past ten years, Chinese people often relied on foreigners for surgery. Although talents have emerged in the last ten years, the general public is still very superstitious about foreigners. Those who study surgery do not have many opportunities to practice surgery abroad, and when they arrive in China, they do not have a place to work because there are too few hospitals. Those who work in hospitals become anonymous because they do not put up signs. Therefore, it is difficult to gain fame, and most of the opportunities to practice are taken away by foreigners. So which surgeon in the city does not also treat internal diseases? As for internal medicine experts, it is very easy to pretend to be one. Even if there are real internal medicine experts who often consult with old doctors for the same disease, they cannot take credit for the effectiveness. Even when the patient is in critical condition, they only bear the responsibility of administering a cardiotonic injection. In Chinese customs, ophthalmology has always been clearly separated from other subjects, so society has a clearer understanding of ophthalmology experts. In addition, the instruments and operations are not available in old ophthalmology, so the business is very developed. Dentistry is in the same position as ophthalmology, but the business of dentists is taken away by silver dentists, so it is not as good as ophthalmology. In the past ten years, obstetrics has indeed been very developed due to the establishment of midwifery schools and the call for affordable obstetrics hospitals. Gynecology is still in a state of contention between the old and the new. Compared with old medicine, the business of new pediatric medicine is simply extremely small. Because new pediatric medicine has many aspects that must rely on nursing, and there are not enough pediatric nurses. Even if there are enough, the patient's family has to bear another burden. If you say to solve it by running a children's hospital, then children staying in hospitals is too far from our country's customs. In addition, except for a few people who have a good understanding of them, the general public does not pay much attention to dermatology, urology, and otolaryngology specialists. Therefore, their business is greatly affected. In order to remedy their business, they have no choice but to take two paths: one is to raise consultation fees and become aristocratic and royal; the other is to treat other diseases. The former is too much of an obstacle to affordable medicine and pharmacy, and the latter is to bury talents. Dermatologists originally always treated venereal diseases, but venereal diseases were divided in half by miscellaneous doctors, and half by general practitioners. By the time patients ask experts for treatment, there are few left, and the disease is too deep, which is often difficult to deal with. After all, there are fewer people in high society who have skin diseases, so raising consultation fees reduces the number of patients to a very low limit.

Saving the Country with Aviation and Saving the Country with Medicine (Part 1) Wang Qizhang

Since the Sino-Japanese War of 1894 and the Boxer Rebellion of 1900, the pain of losing land and humiliating the country has continued year after year, day after day. However, the numb and insensitive government and the people who are drunk and dreaming of death still celebrate peace after the event. Even if there are three or five enlightened people who shout and cry in pain, how can they resist Xue Juzhou, who harmonizes with white snow? Unfortunately, they are also accused of being traitors and suffer misfortune. The author was born later, so he can only learn about the deeds of former people from the elders or read them in biographies. As for the truth at the time, after all, he can only use Mencius's saying that "it is better to have no books than to believe all books" to comfort himself. Speaking of aviation, it has only progressed and developed in the last thirty years. Although I am not an aviator, I have paid close attention to this field and have personally witnessed its gradual improvement and development. Especially the current enemy, Japan, who is bombing our north and south and plundering our land and people, has not been bombed by anyone. They have not launched a nationwide campaign to promote aviation to save the country. They only rely on the saying "be prepared for the worst" and work hard in secret. I admire their national affairs, family affairs, and all actions in society very much. They all have a certain procedure, what should come first, what should come later, what should be expanded, what should be promoted, what should be abolished. Moreover, there are not no backups, or a complete statistic, suddenly raising, suddenly abolishing reckless actions. Therefore, the opposition often has no way to oppose it. In the past, many people who traveled to the East came back and criticized them for being not as good as our Shanghai, not as good as our Beijing, what is not as good as our beautiful and rich; what is not as good as our prosperous and noble. This kind of superficial argument shows that our people do not have a world view and the mentality of improving the steps. Why? Because in the world, no matter which country, which place, which family, which person, has a kind of their own strengths, and also has a kind of their own weaknesses, but the understanding of strengths and weaknesses, each person's vision is different. Eating in front of a ten-foot square, with hundreds of concubines, Mencius does not consider this extravagant to be precious, simple diet, evil clothes, humble palaces, Dayu does not consider this crude to be cheap, each has his own place that he considers precious and cheap, precisely establishing himself to organize his family, and governing the country and pacifying the world, each has their own steps and points of attention. What about Japan? First, he understands himself, his position as an island nation, and he also realizes that he is in the environment of the United States, Russia, and various colonies, and he feels that he lives in the isolation of colored races on earth. So first of all, they focused on national defense for self-defense, and tried their best to expand the navy, first swallowing the islands. He was also afraid that a small island could not survive on its own economically and materially, so he wanted to attack from the weak places around it. Needless to say, China is an economic and material subsidiary outside his government, and he tried his best to focus on industry and commerce to absorb financial resources. He also felt the intense aggressiveness of the European and American countries in the environment, and that everything was isolated and weak, and the danger was extraordinary, so he tried his best to train the army, realize the continental policy, and invade China to strengthen his national power. Therefore, for sixty years, he has followed this step, and for all the domestic supplementary preparations and the development and expansion of foreign forces, he must first deliberate and consider them carefully, and then draw up a budget, and then proceed one by one, distinguishing between the priority and urgency of cutting off the long and making up for the short. Therefore, their roads before the Great Earthquake are really worlds apart from Shanghai. But their kind of bad roads can be passable everywhere in the country, and they can also see the construction of their factory houses, which are simple and rough, narrow and rotten. Compared with our factories, they are really a drop in the bucket, but they can ship goods, supply them domestically, and sell them overseas. And taking their train, the narrow and small situation, at first glance, looks like a toy. It is much better than our domestic, large single-track, magnificent, but it can pass throughout the country, the clock is not wrong, and all materials can be replenished domestically. Also, their clothes, cloth, jewelry, and the like, which one can compare with our beautiful and wealthy, but they deposit the money for this luxury in banks and post offices, or supply it to factories and for national defense, which shows that they have a whole national plan and steps for governing the country, so a small and weak island country, in a few decades, became vigorous and listed among the world's five major powers. This is the result of continuous, year-by-year struggle, the effectiveness of painstaking effort and perseverance, and it is by no means possible to achieve success with a moment of excitement and effort. Now talking about the progress of aviation, everyone already understands, but the achievements of the last twenty years are worth recording, because before, it was a trial period, not a practical time, so there are quite a few records of failures and losses. I don't have time to describe this kind of progress history, so let others say it. But I can say one thing here. Our enemy, Japan, did not invent the plane, nor can he build a plane country, but he understands the trend of the modern world very well, the necessary elements for establishing a country, and the path to follow for competition and survival, so he identified the goal, Lunya, buyya, studiya, doya, put the structure of the plane and the method of driving into it day and night without rest, and painstakingly digging. Those with aspirations among the people sacrificed many lives and money to research, which I saw with my own eyes. Because of poor driving skills or machine failures, I don’t know how many people fell to death and burned to death. Not to mention the establishment and research in the navy and army. If a driver or mechanic dies, they must hold a memorial service to collect pensions and comfort his family, teach and nurture his children, and various rewards to make the drivers have something to rely on and invigorate him. The spirit of hard work and struggle is because airplanes can be bought immediately with money, but talents cannot be bought immediately. If talent can be bought with money, and people's hearts cannot be bought with money, it still won't work, so the realization of saving the country through aviation must have the lasting spirit and patience of Goujian and Wu, in order to solve the two key points of talent cultivation and airplane repair and manufacturing, and then we can achieve the goal of saving the country!

Recent Trends in the Classification Method of Pulmonary Tuberculosis Liu Qijing

General Remarks

In the past, the classification of pulmonary tuberculosis only paid attention to clinical symptoms, and the disease was divided into the first, second, and third stages. Now, in addition to clinical symptoms, attention must also be paid to pathological anatomy, X-ray examination, etc., and lung diseases are divided into chronic (benign) and acute (malignant) types, so the relationship is more complicated. Now, most people still use the terms first, second, and third stages for lung diseases. I am writing this article to introduce this to readers. But before explaining this article, I will first briefly explain the following items: (1) Structure of the Lungs

The lungs are like a large tree. The trunk is the trachea, the large branches are the bronchial tubes, the small branches are the bronchioles, and the smallest branches are the capillaries. The leaves are the alveoli. The function of the leaves is the same as that of the alveoli, and they are the most important part of the new age. The lungs are wrapped in the pleura and are deeply penetrated in several places to separate them, so the right lung is divided into upper, middle, and lower lobes, and the left lung is divided into upper and lower lobes. The shape of the entire lung is like a cone, and the tip is called the apex of the lung. (2) Reasons Why the Apex of the Lung is Prone to Pulmonary Tuberculosis

(1) The upper opening of the chest cavity is a horizontal plane in children. After development, due to the descent of the sternum, it is inclined forward and downward. Therefore, the

Four Major Powers, Britain, France, Italy, and Germany, Cooperate to Maintain 211

Lasting Peace in Europe and the World 212

Britain and France Discuss Revising the Treaty of Versailles 213

Mussolini Plans to Consult with France and Germany 214

Reuters, Rome, 19th: A communique was released today regarding the talks between British Prime Minister MacDonald, Foreign Minister Simon, and Italian Prime Minister Mussolini last night and this afternoon. It stated that the British and Italian authorities, after discussing the general situation, studied a plan to seek understanding on major political issues. This plan was initiated by Mussolini and aims to achieve cooperation between the four major Western powers, Britain, France, Italy, and Germany, in order to enhance the spirit of the Kellogg-Briand Pact and establish a declaration of non-use of force, thereby seeking long-term peace in Europe and the world.

Progress of the Rome Conference 215

Efforts to Resolve Major European Conflicts 216

Rome: British and Italian officials are reluctant to comment further on the precise meaning of the aforementioned Anglo-Italian joint communique. However, it is reported that Mussolini's plan to seek an understanding among the four major powers has been submitted to the French and German ambassadors to Italy for inter-power consultations. The plan will be handled by the heads of the four powers, in the hope of resolving major issues that could trigger significant conflicts in Europe at any time. It is reported that this plan is merely a method of contact and does not contain concrete solutions to the problem. The issue of treaty revision currently occupies a large part of the discussions between British and French authorities, while the issue of arms reduction has barely been discussed. At 6:30 tonight, the British Prime Minister and Foreign Minister paid a 35-minute visit to the Pope. The British officials are scheduled to depart for London tomorrow afternoon, with a brief stopover in Paris.

Havas, Rome, 19th:

During the talks between the British and Italian authorities, the most important point was Mussolini's presentation of a completely unknown plan. Only the preamble to this plan has been discussed by both parties. This plan had been sent to the French government before the meeting between the two sides. What the British officials will discuss with the French authorities after arriving in Paris next Tuesday is this plan, but with British opinions attached. Mussolini's intention is to have the four major powers preside over Europe. Judging from yesterday's meeting, it can be seen that Mussolini's intention is not incompatible with the nature of the League of Nations. Therefore, the main parts of the Italian plan can be used to reform the international organization and make it more solid. This is easier to do after Japan left Geneva, because the remaining permanent members of the Executive Council are only four countries, and these four countries are the four major countries referred to in the Italian plan. As for the remaining countries, the British cabinet does not intend to exclude them from participating, but if the major countries can reach a compromise first, then the remaining countries will be more easily amenable. In addition, Britain is quite reactive to German Chancellor Hitler's violence. The Italian Prime Minister is well aware of this, so he will use a friendly attitude to advise Germany in order to reassure Britain.

Communiqué of the Italian Government 217

MacDonald Leaves Rome for Paris Today 218

Havas, Rome, 19th: British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon held talks with the Italian Prime Minister yesterday and today. The government has just released a communiqué stating that the Prime Minister met with British Prime Minister MacDonald and Foreign Minister Simon at the Palazzo Venezia from 6:00 p.m. to 7:30 p.m. yesterday. This afternoon, from 2:30 p.m. to 4:00 p.m., they met again at the British Embassy. After exchanging detailed views on the overall situation, both sides studied a compromise plan on various major issues. This plan was drafted by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini and is intended to enable the four major Western powers to cooperate with each other in order to maintain long-term peace in Europe and the world in accordance with the spirit of the Kellogg-Briand Pact and the declaration prohibiting the use of force. The British cabinet members are scheduled to depart from Rome for London tomorrow, with a slight delay in Paris in order to meet with French authorities.

Nanjing: For the transport of Guangdong salt to Hunan, hundreds of thousands of small merchants and porters have traditionally relied on carrying the salt into the province for a living. However, the Taili Heji Company signed a contract with the Hunan and Guangdong authorities to monopolize the transport and sale of salt, and the salt commissioners of the two provinces also approved a trial implementation of the scheme, resulting in the loss of jobs for a large number of people. Representatives were sent to Nanjing to petition and appeal to various parties before the year, but with no results. Members of the Central Committee from Hunan, Tang Shengzhi, Tang Youqian, He Yaozu, Wang Qi, Guo Chuntao, Deng Feihuang, etc., recently sent a joint letter to Finance Minister Song, stating that the Guangdong salt monopoly case has been pending for half a year and has not been resolved. The Hunan Provincial Government has not implemented it due to strong public opposition. The Taili Company even lobbied the Guangdong salt commissioners to allow them to start operations in Guangdong Province first. Recently, disputes have arisen in the border counties of Hunan Province, such as the severance of salt distribution and the economic alienation of the people in the two provinces, resulting in a serious situation. At this time of national crisis, with the flames of war burning fiercely, failure to quickly provide relief may trigger a disturbance. This case concerns the livelihoods of millions of people and the safety of thousands of miles of territory. They requested that the trial implementation order be swiftly revoked in order to maintain the people's livelihood and quell the source of the unrest, etc. (Morning of 20th Central News Agency)

Tianjin French Municipal Council 245

Forcibly Takes Over Beiyang Hospital 246

Sales Contract Established on January 15th 247

Hospital Director Zhang Zixiang Ordered to Refuse to Hand Over 248

Tianjin: Beiyang Hospital covers an estimated 39 mu of land and was founded by Li Hongzhang 52 years ago. It is well-equipped. It used to be under the jurisdiction of the Navy Department, but in the last five or six years, the Navy Department stopped providing funding, and the hospital's operations fell into difficulty. The hospital's doctors and staff, totaling more than 30 people, rely solely on registration fees to purchase medicines and food, and there is no salary. Last year, more than 50,000 poor people were treated. Foreign doctors resigned and went elsewhere due to the lack of salary. 14 years ago, a Frenchman named Kou was a doctor at the hospital. Kou had a small steamship that was being repaired at the Dagu Shipyard and was unfortunately destroyed. Kou returned to his country the year before last and independently priced the ship at 140,000 yuan and filed it with the French Consulate. Last winter, a certain authority sold the hospital to the French Municipal Council, and the contract was established on January 15. The Chinese signatory was so-and-so, and the French signatory was Consul General Nabos. The price per mu was 20,000 taels, totaling 780,000 taels. There are two buildings next to the hospital, which were early foreign doctors' dormitories. This time, the French Municipal Council depreciated them for 140,000 yuan to compensate for Kou's ship losses. The French Municipal Council took over the two buildings on the 18th. Hospital Director Zhang Zixiang was ordered by the Navy Department not to hand over the keys. The Municipal Council immediately sent personnel to break open the doors and forcibly take over. The Municipal Council has scheduled to take over the entire hospital property on the 25th and has issued a notice to vacate. If they do not vacate by the deadline, they will forcibly take over. Director Zhang, who is empty-handed, is afraid that he will not be able to resist. It is reported that the hospital owes foreign medical expenses of no more than 200,000 yuan. During the time of Chu Yupu, there was an attempt to sell it, but the sale was stopped due to opposition from the citizens. Now it has become a reality. Alas, the die is cast, and opposition is ineffective. What a pity! (20th Dispatch)

Luo and Chiang Pass Through Jinan and Return to Nanjing 249

Issue Important Statements 250

Jinan Correspondence: After Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went north, Foreign Minister Luo Wengan also came north from Nanjing. He met Chiang Kai-shek in Shijiazhuang to discuss diplomatic policy towards Japan. After completing his official duties, he went to Beiping to meet with envoys from various countries, declaring China's future diplomatic policy towards Japan. He stated that if Japanese troops disturb Tianjin and Beiping, harming the rights of third countries, China will not be responsible. He also strongly refuted rumors of direct Sino-Japanese negotiations in order to avoid confusing the international community. In addition, after returning to China, Ambassador to Japan Chiang Zuobin also went to Baoding a few days ago to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to report on the recent situation in Japan. He then went to Beiping to meet with Luo. Because Luo had completed his work and there were many accumulated events in the ministry awaiting handling, he took the No. 202 express train back to Nanjing with Chiang Zuobin last night. This morning (the 17th) at 9:00 a.m., the train passed through Jinan. Provincial Chairman Han Fuju, Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun, Industry Director Wang Fangting, Provincial Committee Member Zhang Weicun, Provincial Secretary General Zhang Shaotang, and Higher Court President Wu Zhenzan all went to the station to welcome them. Luo and Chiang did not get off the train and met with Han and others on the train, and also met with various reporters, talking for a long time. At 9:30 a.m., Luo and Chiang's special train went south. Luo and Chiang's statements are recorded separately below:

#### Luo Wengan's Statement

The reporter first interviewed Luo and made the following statement:

(Question) How did the Minister meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek to discuss the general direction of diplomatic policy towards Japan?

(Answer) I have made many statements in Beiping and Tianjin, and most of them have been disclosed in various newspapers. There is no other news to tell you.

(Question) What new avenues are there for Sino-Japanese diplomacy?

(Answer) Last month, the League of Nations passed a report and organized an advisory committee, inviting the United States and Russia to join in discussing the Sino-Japanese dispute. The United States has sent a representative to participate. Although Russia has not joined, it has expressed considerable sympathy for us. The advisory committee held a meeting on Wednesday to discuss the Sino-Japanese incident, and there will be new developments in the future.

(Question) After the Minister returns to Nanjing this time, will he come north again soon?

(Answer) I am returning to Nanjing to deal with the backlog of events in the ministry, so I probably won't be able to come north recently.

(Question) After the Minister arrives in Nanjing, will he go to Shanghai to meet President Wang?

(Answer) President Wang is arriving in Nanjing from Shanghai, and I won't have time when I arrive in Nanjing.

(Question) What is the recent battle situation at the front?

(Answer) Our army, Song Zheyuan's troops, have annihilated many enemies at Xifengkou, and the battle situation at Lengkou is also very good.

(Question) Is Chairman Chiang Kai-shek returning south soon?

(Answer) Chairman Chiang Kai-shek may not return south recently.

Then Luo had a cordial conversation with the various dignitaries who welcomed him, and said that Chairman Chiang Kai-shek insisted on resisting to the end, and that external reports that he would negotiate directly were absolutely untrue. Direct negotiations are what the enemy hopes for, using heavy troops to pressure us on the one hand, and spreading rumors on the other, to entice us with sweet words, with the intention of promoting direct negotiations. Little do they know that even if our country resists and is defeated, we will never surrender. Although the League of Nations is helping our country, we cannot rely on it, but we must never privately compromise with Japan. This principle is very clear and does not need to be argued. I once declared to the Japanese that even if China is defeated and retreats south of the Yellow River because of resistance, it will still resist to the end.

#### Chiang Zuobin's Statement

After the reporter talked with Luo, he interviewed Chiang Zuobin. They talked to each other as follows:

(Question) What is the Ambassador's opinion on the current Sino-Japanese diplomacy?

(Answer) Minister Luo has already talked about this to you just now. Because of my position, I am sorry that I cannot express my opinion.

(Question) Will the Ambassador return to Japan soon?

(Answer) Under these current circumstances, of course I cannot return to Japan.

(Question) What is the general situation in Japan?

(Answer) The situation in Japan is quite complicated. Broadly speaking, it can be divided into two factions: one is the radical faction, consisting of ambitious young people and young soldiers, who advocate invading China and expanding territory. Since occupying our Northeast, their arrogance has become more and more rampant, and they will not hesitate to start a world war. The second is the moderate faction, consisting of the Japanese people, intellectuals, capitalists, and experienced strategists. In their view, although Japan has occupied the Northeast and offended the League of Nations, it is a failure rather than a victory, a shame rather than an honor. They are worried and feel the danger of the country's fortune. However, the radical faction's aggressive proposals have now occupied four provinces and achieved great victories, and are worshiped by the majority of people, so the moderate faction is silent and dare not speak. Their finances are extremely chaotic and fearful, but because the country's organization is strict, they are currently trying to maintain it, but I am afraid that there will be a day when it cannot be sustained. (17th)
